# BrainWise System Architecture Reference

> **LATEST ENTRY: v144 (Session 143 CLOSE)** - Lesson Experience uplift Phase 3 continues: INT-4 the `reveal_cards` interactive lesson-block type (a responsive GRID of click-to-flip two-face cards), STATELESS (no table/RPC for the block; completion via the existing sticky `upsert_lesson_block_progress` path; all cards revealed completes, an empty `items` block auto-completes, `gating_required` defaults false). Two migrations (`lesson_block_types` row; `_walk_block_config_for_asset_refs` extended with the `items[]`/`front_image_asset_id` branch), NO new edge fn, and full §61 5-surface parity (`draft-lesson-block` v18, `scaffold-lesson-outline` v29, `expand-lesson-from-outline` v30; `ai-authoring-chat` exempt). Front AND back are independently brandable; the per-card image follows the flashcards author-upload model (no AiPane/vision change). Doc-correction recorded: the live flashcards block uses `cards[N].front_image_asset_id` (earlier docs said `back_image_asset_id`); reveal_cards matches it. PRIOR: v143 INT-3 hotspot; v142 VIS-3 + VIS-6 (frontend-only Phase 2 close); v141 INT-1 open_response. The v144 entry is at the top of the changelog directly below this header; v143 (hotspot) is next, then v142, then v141, then the newest-first v138/v139/v140 cluster (slightly out of order).

*v144 - Session 143 CLOSE. **Lesson Experience uplift Phase 3 continues: INT-4 the `reveal_cards` interactive lesson-block type lands as a STATELESS grid-of-click-to-flip-cards block, with full §61 5-surface parity. Two migrations, NO new edge fn, three generators versioned, one Lovable frontend arc. No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold; §61 5-surface parity reaffirmed MANDATORY per new block type).** **REVEAL_CARDS BLOCK (durable).** A responsive GRID of two-face cards; the learner CLICKS a card to flip it (3D flip) from its front to its back, and revealing every card completes the block. An optional authored instruction line sits above the grid. STATELESS by design - like INT-3 hotspot (and unlike INT-1 open_response, which has a per-attempt table) reveal_cards needs NO dedicated table and NO block-specific RPC: completion rides the existing sticky onBlockComplete -> reportProgress -> upsert_lesson_block_progress path (all cards revealed in-session completes; an empty `items` block auto-completes), gating_required defaults false. Icon `Eye`. DESIGN LOCK (durable): reveal_cards is a quick reveal GRID, deliberately NOT flashcards (the one-at-a-time recall carousel with Got it/Review again self-rating) and NOT an accordion (titled long-form reference sections); it was chosen as its own type for risk isolation rather than overloading flashcards. **CONFIG SCHEMA is FLAT, array key `items`, and the per-card image field name `front_image_asset_id` MATCHES the live flashcards block:** { instructions, items:[{client_id, front(TipTap doc), front_image_asset_id(uuid|null), front_caption(plain text|null), back(TipTap doc), front_color(brand hex|null), back_color(brand hex|null)}], gating_required, background_color, padding }. Each card carries a TipTap front + optional front image + optional caption and a TipTap back. **Front AND back are INDEPENDENTLY brandable** (front_color/back_color are saturated brand hexes; the renderer derives readable text per face via the existing readableTextColorForBg luminance helper, NOT a fixed pairing table). The per-card image follows the FLASHCARDS pattern (author uploads post-generation; the AI generators emit front_image_asset_id null; NO AiPane outline-stage image-resolution and NO vision change - this is the key contrast with INT-3 hotspot, which rides the AiPane image_resolved path). **MIGRATIONS (durable, each verified by a separate execute_sql).** (1) seed_reveal_cards_lesson_block_type: public.lesson_block_types row block_type='reveal_cards' (category 'interactive', is_interactive true, is_scored false, is_v1_active true); replace_lesson_blocks validates against this table, save_lesson_block_draft + upsert_lesson_block_progress are type-agnostic. (2) add_reveal_cards_to_asset_ref_walker: CREATE OR REPLACE public._walk_block_config_for_asset_refs added the reveal_cards branch walking config.items[] emitting each item's front_image_asset_id. KEY ARCHITECTURE FACT (durable, re-confirmed): all three asset RPCs (content_asset_refs tracking, editor get-lesson-block-asset-urls signing, trainee get_lesson_block_assets_for_trainee signing) route through this ONE walker, so the single branch edit covers ref-tracking AND both signing paths - the §60/§61 asset-parity mechanism (same as flashcards' cards[]/front_image_asset_id branch and hotspot's hotspot_asset branch). No new table this session (stateless block); NOTIFY pgrst run. **NO new edge fn this session** (reveal_cards needs no vision/feedback fn; contrast INT-1's lesson-open-response-feedback and INT-3's lesson-hotspot-autoplace). **FRONTEND (durable, one Lovable arc, GitHub-API SHA-verified, CDN cross-checked per §117).** Main HEAD 5a9e62c0614c340a7ae24de3366f9d29c99f2382 (baseline d6c9c695). Five surfaces under src/components/super-admin/lesson-blocks/: blockTypeMeta.ts (blob 67012123; Eye import + 'reveal_cards' in the BlockType union + BLOCK_TYPE_META with defaultConfig front/back emptyDoc + front_image_asset_id/front_caption/front_color/back_color/instructions/gating + IN_SCOPE_BLOCK_TYPES; AddBlockPopover is dynamic off these so no picker edit); NEW block-forms/RevealCardsBlockForm.tsx (blob 407bc6dc; per-card front RichTextEditor + reused Pexels+upload picker [FileUploadField] + front_caption + back RichTextEditor + front/back BrandColorSwatch; instructions field; gating Switch; its emit spreads `...value` FIRST so block-level background_color/padding survive); BlockEditorPane.tsx (blob 1f7333f2; dispatch); BlockRenderer.tsx (blob 224f3291; `case "reveal_cards"` -> RevealCardsRender; ALL hooks [useState/useRef/useEffect] precede the `items.length===0` early return per §137; 3D CSS flip; savedProgress seeds the revealed set + completionFiredRef; trainee-gated completion with empty=auto-complete; custom face colors routed through the local readableTextColorForBg, defaulting to brand CSS vars); lesson-blocks.css (blob 5786eb77; `=== Session 143: reveal_cards ===` grid + 3D flip transforms + prefers-reduced-motion guard). One inert cosmetic nit noted (non-blocking): the card className renders a trailing space when not revealed (`bw-reveal-card `). **§61 AI-AUTHORING PARITY (durable, all three dashboard-paste, reproduced full from get_edge_function since the app repo lacks these fns, esbuild parse-clean, verify_jwt FALSE, boot-probed OPTIONS 204 + no-auth POST 401).** draft-lesson-block v18: BLOCK_SCHEMAS.reveal_cards (2-12 cards; front/back markdown; front_image_asset_id null in AI output; front_caption optional <=80 chars; front_color/back_color null in AI output [author picks post-generation]; instructions optional; do NOT emit completion/progress) + a transformConfigForCanvas case (instructions; items mapped to client_id uuid + front/back via mdToTipTap + front_image_asset_id null + front_caption + front_color/back_color via BRAND_COLORS.has() + gating_required false default); the two system-prompt lines extended so the image-null list names reveal_cards.items[N].front_image_asset_id and the color-null list names reveal_cards.items[N].front_color/back_color (21 BLOCK_SCHEMAS keys, 21 transform cases). scaffold-lesson-outline v29: 'reveal_cards' in ALLOWED_BLOCK_TYPES + one intent-guide bullet that bakes in the flashcards-vs-accordion differentiation (21 allowed types). expand-lesson-from-outline v30: 'reveal_cards' in ALLOWED_BLOCK_TYPES + BLOCK_SCHEMA_HINTS.reveal_cards + a transformConfigForCanvas case using the brand-aware isAllowed(brand, front_color/back_color) + a builder rule; the generic post-transform background tinting (skip divider + callout) already covers the reveal_cards block-level background_color (21 schema hints, 21 transform cases); brand section / windowing / toTint intact. ai-authoring-chat EXEMPT from §61 (type-agnostic at code + data level, per the v141 rationale). **DOC-CORRECTION (durable).** The live flashcards block uses cards[N].front_image_asset_id (the image sits on the card FRONT, per the Session-67 flip); earlier docs in places said back_image_asset_id. reveal_cards deliberately matches the flashcards field name front_image_asset_id so the walker branch + the generator transforms read identically. **CANDIDATE FIX LOGGED (durable, not actioned).** FlashcardsBlockForm's emit returns only { cards, gating_required }, dropping any top-level background_color/padding the block carried (a latent config-drop bug); RevealCardsBlockForm avoids it by spreading `...value` first before overlaying its fields. Fix flashcards in a future arc. **VERIFICATION.** All three generators boot-probed (OPTIONS 204 + no-auth POST 401 missing_bearer_token); frontend at main 5a9e62c0, every changed file's git-hash-object matched the GitHub API blob SHA (CDN cross-checked per §117) with wiring grep-confirmed; both migrations verified by separate execute_sql. **Edge fn versions: draft-lesson-block v18, scaffold-lesson-outline v29, expand-lesson-from-outline v30; ai-authoring-chat unchanged at v14; no new edge fn. No cron; no RLS change (stateless block, no new table); ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched.** Cole will run a full smoke test of ALL lesson-block changes at once next session (chat scaffold->expand builds reveal_cards with front/back, no image, colors null; per-block Refine via draft-lesson-block; branded-face legibility; plus the carried INT-1 + INT-3 live tests). PHASE 3 remaining: INT-5 drag-to-order (precedent card_sort dnd-kit + knowledge_check ranking/timeline; decide own block vs ranking-wrapper, stateless vs stored) then INT-8 activation poll (lesson-cover-level, heaviest; decide cover-vs-block + response storage). Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v149, this v144 entry, session-143-to-144.md.*

*v143 - Session 142 CLOSE. **Lesson Experience uplift Phase 3 STARTED: INT-3 the `hotspot` interactive lesson-block type lands as a STATELESS labeled-image-with-clickable-markers block, with full §61 5-surface parity and a new Opus vision auto-place edge fn. Three migrations, one new edge fn, three generators versioned, two frontend commits. No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold; §61 5-surface parity reaffirmed MANDATORY per new block type).** **HOTSPOT BLOCK (durable).** A labeled image carrying 2-12 clickable markers; clicking a marker opens a Popover revealing its label + a short TipTap note. STATELESS by design - unlike INT-1 open_response (per-attempt table) the hotspot block needs NO dedicated table and NO block-specific RPC: completion rides the existing sticky onBlockComplete -> reportProgress -> upsert_lesson_block_progress path (opening all markers in-session completes; an empty-hotspots block auto-completes), gating_required defaults false. CONFIG SCHEMA is FLAT, matching the image block: { asset_id, alt, attribution, instructions, hotspots:[{client_id, x(0-100 percent), y(0-100 percent), label(plain text), content(TipTap doc)}], gating_required, background_color, padding }. Marker x/y are 0-100 percentages of the image box. **MIGRATIONS (durable, each verified by a separate execute_sql).** (1) seed_hotspot_lesson_block_type: public.lesson_block_types row block_type='hotspot' (category 'interactive', is_interactive true, is_scored false, is_v1_active true); replace_lesson_blocks validates against this table, save_lesson_block_draft + upsert_lesson_block_progress are type-agnostic. (2) add_hotspot_to_asset_ref_walker: CREATE OR REPLACE public._walk_block_config_for_asset_refs added 'hotspot' to the single-asset IN-list emitting ref_field 'hotspot_asset'. KEY ARCHITECTURE FACT (durable): all three asset RPCs (content_asset_refs tracking, editor get-lesson-block-asset-urls signing, trainee get_lesson_block_assets_for_trainee signing) route through this ONE walker, so the single IN-list edit covers ref-tracking AND both signing paths - this is the §60/§61 asset-parity mechanism for any new single-image block type. (3) create_lesson_hotspot_autoplace_log: rate-limit table public.lesson_hotspot_autoplace_log (id uuid pk gen_random_uuid(), user_id uuid not null, content_item_id uuid, created_at timestamptz default now(); index (user_id, created_at DESC); RLS ENABLED; REVOKE ALL FROM authenticated,anon per §157). Only new table this session; justifies the 10/hr vision rate limit (no generic rate-limit helper exists - pg_proc checked). **NEW EDGE FN lesson-hotspot-autoplace v1 (durable, verify_jwt TRUE, function id d70c4cd7).** Class A auth pattern: getClaims + super-admin account_type='brainwise_super_admin' check + enforceImpersonationGate('permission_change'); _shared/impersonation_gate.ts byte-copied from lesson-ingest-pexels-asset. Input { content_item_id, asset_id, hotspots:[{client_id, label, content_text?}] }. Flow: count lesson_hotspot_autoplace_log rows in the last hour (>=10 -> 429) then insert a log row; resolve the asset via serviceClient.rpc get_lesson_block_assets(p_content_item_id, p_extra_asset_ids:[asset_id]) -> out_bucket/out_path; storage download; base64 (jsr:@std/encoding@1/base64); ONE Opus vision call (claude-opus-4-7, x-api-key + anthropic-version 2023-06-01, image base64 + text asking for strict JSON [{client_id,x,y}]); clamp x/y to 0-100, keep only known client_ids; return {placements, model}. MAX_IMAGE_BYTES 5MB; media type from path extension. Boot-probed OPTIONS 204 + no-auth POST 401. **TWO-SEQUENTIAL-OPUS RULE NOT VIOLATED:** this fn makes a single Opus call; the generators make their own single calls; nothing bundles two Opus calls in one fn (the 150s ceiling rule holds). **FRONTEND (durable, two Lovable commits, GitHub-API SHA-verified, CDN cross-checked per §117).** Prompt 1 (main c67caf40, §61 surfaces 2+3): blockTypeMeta.ts (Target icon + 'hotspot' in the BlockType union + BLOCK_TYPE_META + IN_SCOPE_BLOCK_TYPES; AddBlockPopover is dynamic off these so no picker edit); NEW block-forms/HotspotBlockForm.tsx (reuses the Pexels+upload picker via FileUploadField refField='image_asset' -> newsletter-image-search -> lesson-ingest-pexels-asset, registerNewAssetId via useLessonBlockAssetUrls; click-to-place bw-hotspot-canvas clamps 0-100; numbered markers with stopPropagation; 12 cap, <2 advisory; numeric x/y inputs; RichTextEditor content; gating Switch); BlockEditorPane.tsx dispatch; BlockRenderer.tsx (Popover import; case 'hotspot' -> HotspotRender with ALL hooks before the early return per §137; savedProgress seeds the opened set + completionFiredRef; trainee-gated completion with empty=auto-complete; Popover onOpenChange adds to the opened set; PopoverContent themed via var(--lesson-surface)/--lesson-primary and .bw-image-attribution); lesson-blocks.css (bw-hotspot-canvas, bw-hotspot-marker, prefers-reduced-motion guard). Prompt 2 (main d6c9c695): HotspotBlockForm.tsx gained Wand2 + a module-scope tiptapToPlainText(doc) helper + autoPlacing state + runAutoPlace() invoking supabase.functions.invoke('lesson-hotspot-autoplace',{content_item_id, asset_id, hotspots:[{client_id,label,content_text:tiptapToPlainText(content)}]}) then applying returned placements by client_id (clamp 0-100), behind an "Auto-place with AI" button disabled until autoPlacing || !asset_id || hotspots.length===0 || !contentItemId; ai-pane/Stage2Outline.tsx broadened two conditions to (block_type==='image' || block_type==='hotspot') so hotspot is image-bearing at outline review (approval gating + ImageResolutionSection render); ai-pane/AiPane.tsx broadened the stitch condition to set config.asset_id + config.attribution + onRegisterAsset for hotspot. types.ts unchanged. **AiPane IMAGE-RESOLUTION PATH (durable):** OutlineItem carries image_query / image_resolved{asset_id,attribution,thumb_url} / image_skipped; the outline cannot be approved until each image-bearing item is resolved or skipped; on build the resolved asset (asset_id + attribution) is stitched onto the block by outline index. Hotspot now uses this SAME path as the image block; the walker change tracks the hotspot_asset ref on save. **§61 AI-AUTHORING PARITY (durable, all three dashboard-paste, reproduced full from get_edge_function since the app repo lacks these fns, esbuild-clean, verify_jwt FALSE, boot-probed OPTIONS 204 + no-auth POST 401).** draft-lesson-block v17: BLOCK_SCHEMAS.hotspot (author uploads image so asset_id null; alt 5-15 words; hotspots 2-12 with label plain 1-5 words + content_markdown inline-only; do NOT emit x/y/asset_id/client_id/attribution/gating_required) + transformConfigForCanvas case 'hotspot' (asset_id:null, attribution:null, instructions, hotspots with client_id uuid + placeholder x=Math.round((i+1)/(n+1)*100) + y= i%2?60:40 + label + content via mdToTipTap, gating_required:false); NO image_query (its image block is author-upload too). scaffold-lesson-outline v28: 'hotspot' in ALLOWED_BLOCK_TYPES + one intent-guide bullet (20 bullets). expand-lesson-from-outline v29: 'hotspot' in ALLOWED_BLOCK_TYPES + BLOCK_SCHEMA_HINTS.hotspot + transformConfigForCanvas case 'hotspot' (same placeholder-coords shape) + a builder rule; the generic post-transform background tinting already covers hotspot (neither divider nor callout); brand section / windowing / toTint intact (20 transform cases). **DESIGN LOCK (durable):** the text generators emit hotspot label + content but PLACEHOLDER marker coords (even x-spread, staggered y), NOT image-accurate; accurate placement comes only from the vision auto-place button or manual drag. draft-lesson-block does NOT resolve an image (author uploads). **SUPERSEDED DECISION (durable):** an earlier "generators emit image_query" plan was overturned after reading the code - expand's image block emits asset_id:null and images resolve at the OUTLINE stage in AiPane via image_resolved then stitch onto the block; no image_query field exists, so hotspot reuses that path rather than inventing a new field. **VERIFICATION:** all three generators boot-probed; frontend prompt 1 at main c67caf40 and prompt 2 at main d6c9c695, every changed file hash-matched the GitHub API blob SHAs (CDN cross-checked per §117) with wiring grep-confirmed. **Edge fn versions: lesson-hotspot-autoplace v1 NEW, draft-lesson-block v17, scaffold-lesson-outline v28, expand-lesson-from-outline v29; ai-authoring-chat unchanged at v14. No cron; RLS only on lesson_hotspot_autoplace_log; ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched.** PHASE 3 STARTED (INT-3 hotspot). Remaining Phase 3: INT-4 click-to-reveal, INT-5 drag-to-order, INT-8 activation poll. Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v148, this v143 entry, session-142-to-143.md.*

*v142 - Session 141 CLOSE. **Lesson Experience uplift Phase 2 COMPLETE: VIS-3 and VIS-6 land as a render-time, brand-driven cover/viewer treatment and a static end-of-lesson recap + completion moment. Entirely frontend on the v140 brand-var layer; no schema, RPC, edge function, migration, cron, or RLS change; no new block type (so §61 not triggered). No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold).** **VIS-3 BRAND-TEXTURED COVER + BRANDED VIEWER CHROME (durable).** Decision: NO stock-photo hero. Cole rejected stock imagery (cheapness + dating risk) and the private-bucket/signing fork that reusing lesson-ingest-pexels-asset for a public cover would require; the hero is instead a CSS brand-texture derived entirely from existing lesson_brands color slots via color-mix (already used in the block CSS), so zero new data. COVER (LessonTitleCard.tsx, shared by viewer + editor preview): the hero band background went from a solid var(--cover-primary) to a dark-anchored linear-gradient(135deg, var(--cover-primary), color-mix toward #000 ~18%) layered under a radial var(--cover-accent) glow, with a faint BrainWise spiral watermark (the existing BrainWiseMark, absolute, opacity 0.06) behind a relative z-10 content wrapper; white text kept (dark-anchored so legibility holds on any brand; readableTextColorForBg deliberately NOT pulled in). SECTION BAND (LessonBlockViewer.tsx): the literal rgba(2,31,54,0.06) navy tint became a soft color-mix gradient of var(--lesson-primary) toward var(--lesson-surface) (9%->4%), the left rule moved from global var(--bw-orange) to var(--lesson-cta), and the numbered badge from bg-[var(--bw-orange)] to bg-[var(--lesson-cta)]. VIEWER CHROME: the four remaining global --bw-orange elements (TOC progress bar fill, TOC active-entry dot, Continue button, Complete-lesson button) all moved to var(--lesson-cta); the two buttons switched from a Tailwind bracket bg + hover:bg-[--bw-orange-600] to inline backgroundColor var(--lesson-cta) + hover:opacity-90 (the cover Start-button pattern, avoids a -600 hover shade). MOBILE-PORTAL FACT (durable): the mobile TOC renders in a Radix Sheet that portals to document root, escaping the style={lessonBrandVars} wrapper; --bw-orange resolved there only because it is a :root token, so the mobile SheetContent now carries style={lessonBrandVars} itself so --lesson-* resolve inside the portal. NET (durable): --bw-orange is fully eliminated from the lesson viewer; ALL cover + band + viewer-chrome theming now reads lesson_brands through the v140 brand-var layer (--cover-* set on the cover root from the cover's own lesson_brands query; --lesson-* set on the viewer main-return wrapper from the viewer's lesson_brands query), falling back to BrainWise navy/orange only when no brand row or a null slot. KEEP-FIXED (durable, reaffirmed): --bw-forest (success/done/correct), the other semantic status colors, and readableTextColorForBg stay literal; they are status/contrast, not brand. **VIS-6 STATIC RECAP + COMPLETION MOMENT + SECTION REWARD (durable).** Decision: static recap (A), inline completion card (i), both lesson-end and section-level; AI recap deferred to Track 5. KEY FACT (durable): finishing a single content_item lesson had NO completion moment - the ContentItemViewer cascade celebration modal only fires at module/curriculum/certification tiers (openCascade skips tier='content_item'); the lesson level had only a quiet inline 'Lesson complete.' banner. VIS-6 (all in LessonBlockViewer.tsx, no new imports, reuses bw-section-enter, no BlockRenderer/CSS change): (1) the banner became a COMPLETION CARD on the final section when isCompleted - forest success header (var(--font-display)), 'You finished {title}', a recap list titled 'What you can now do' from content_items.outcomes (parent-merged onto contentItem) else 'What you covered' from the heading topics (buildLessonToc), hidden if neither, plus stat chips (sections count, passedChecks/totalChecks from knowledge_check intersect completedIds, ~totalMinutes from estimateMinutes(blocks)); Previous + Start-again actions preserved; success=forest semantic, accent label=--lesson-accent, checks=--lesson-cta. (2) a forest 'Section complete' reward PILL in each section footer, shown when completedSections.has(currentSectionIdx) && !(isFinalSection && isCompleted), with the bw-section-enter (prefers-reduced-motion-guarded) entrance. DESIGN LOCK (durable): the single footer pill covers BOTH the scope's section-completion AND gated-block-clearance triggers, because clearing the last gating-required block is exactly what flips a section to complete (completedSections = visited AND all gating-required blocks done), and footer placement makes it feel earned for no-gating sections; per-block toasts/confetti were deliberately rejected as noisy. The lesson-tier completion moment is intentionally inline (NOT a modal) to avoid stacking under the module/curriculum cascade modal. VERIFICATION: main commit fa9e2f7f; LessonTitleCard.tsx blob ad25a8c8, LessonBlockViewer.tsx blob 6c7737b7 (API-authoritative, matched git-hash-object of raw@main -> CDN confirmed fresh, per §117). **Edge fn / cron / RLS / schema: none changed; ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched.** PHASE 2 COMPLETE (INT-1 S140 + VIS-3 + VIS-6 S141). Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v147, this v142 entry, session-141-to-142.md.*

*v141 - Session 140 CLOSE. **Lesson Experience uplift Phase 2: the open_response AI-feedback lesson-block type (INT-1) lands as new schema + a new edge function + frontend, and §61 block-type parity is reaffirmed as MANDATORY across the three lesson-authoring generators. No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold; §61 reaffirmed).** **OPEN_RESPONSE BLOCK (durable).** A new interactive lesson-block type: the learner writes free text and receives AI formative coaching with NO score and NO correct answer (distinct from knowledge_check, which is right/wrong and defaults gating_required true). Storage is a DEDICATED table public.lesson_open_responses (per-attempt: id, user_id, content_item_id, block_id, attempt_number, response_text, ai_feedback, model, created_at; UNIQUE(user_id,block_id,attempt_number); FK cascades), chosen over a progress JSON blob so attempts are retained and mentor-reviewable. RLS = own + super-admin + active-mentor SELECT, service_role ALL; the table is treated as secret-bearing (REVOKE ALL FROM authenticated,anon then explicit grants, per §157). AUTH MODEL (durable): the feedback edge function lesson-open-response-feedback v1 is verify_jwt TRUE and authorizes through a SECDEF gate _authorize_lesson_block_for_trainee(p_block_id,p_user_id default null), a byte-copy of the live lesson-asset authorization gate (LMS module entitlement + self/super-admin/active-mentor + published non-archived lesson + active/completed user_curriculum_assignments); the gate is internal-only (postgres+service_role, REVOKE authenticated). The two writer RPCs prepare_lesson_open_response(p_block_id) and record_lesson_open_response(p_block_id,p_response_text,p_ai_feedback,p_model default null) are SECDEF authenticated+service_role, run the impersonation gate, enforce a 10/hr rate limit, and insert attempt-numbered rows. The edge function makes a SINGLE Opus call (claude-opus-4-7, x-api-key + anthropic-version 2023-06-01) and returns formative coaching text only. lesson_block_types gained the open_response row (category interactive, is_scored false, is_v1_active true); replace_lesson_blocks validates block_type against that table, while save_lesson_block_draft and upsert_lesson_block_progress are type-agnostic. COMPLETION MODEL (durable): submit-once marks the block complete via the existing onBlockComplete -> reportProgress -> upsert_lesson_block_progress path; gating_required defaults FALSE (author-overridable); completion is sticky. RENDERER (durable): the trainee renderer passes blockClientId straight to the edge function as block_id because in trainee mode EditorBlock.client_id === the DB lesson_blocks.id; editor mode renders a disabled preview; all hooks precede the editor-mode early return (§137); styling uses the per-lesson brand vars from the v140 brand-var layer, no literal brand hexes. **§61 PARITY IS MANDATORY (durable, reaffirmed; Cole directive).** Every new lesson-block type must be added, in the same arc it ships, to ALL THREE lesson-authoring generators: draft-lesson-block (per-block Refine-with-AI iterator), scaffold-lesson-outline (outline proposer; the fn that actually puts a type into an outline), and expand-lesson-from-outline (outline builder). For open_response: draft-lesson-block v16 (BLOCK_SCHEMAS.open_response + a transformConfigForCanvas case), scaffold-lesson-outline v27 (ALLOWED_BLOCK_TYPES + intent-guide bullet), expand-lesson-from-outline v28 (ALLOWED_BLOCK_TYPES + a BLOCK_SCHEMA_HINTS entry + a transformConfigForCanvas case + a builder rule; the generic post-transform background tinting already covers it since it is neither divider nor callout). DELIVERY FACT (durable): these three are dashboard-paste (over the MCP inline size limit) and the app repo supabase/functions/ does NOT contain them, so they must be reproduced FULL from the deployed get_edge_function source, syntax-checked (esbuild parse), deployed via the Supabase dashboard with verify_jwt false, then boot-probed (OPTIONS 204 + no-auth POST 401 missing_bearer_token confirms compile + boot + the internal getClaims gate). **ai-authoring-chat IS EXEMPT FROM §61 (durable rationale).** The Stage-1 conversational co-pilot (v14) has no block-type enumeration in code; its only source of block awareness is the ai_authoring_context table, and the active lesson-authoring rows there (platform_overview, framework_terminology, scientific_foundations, output_format_rules, guardrails) enumerate ZERO block types (only the newsletter_html_authoring_spec row mentions any, and it is the newsletter spec). It is type-agnostic at the code AND data level and does not generate the outline (scaffold does), so it needs no change when a block type is added. Making the co-pilot proactively suggest specific block types (e.g. reflections) would require adding a FULL block catalog to ai_authoring_context, which is a product enhancement, not a parity obligation. INCIDENTAL (flagged, not actioned): every lesson-authoring fn currently loads ALL active ai_authoring_context rows, including the ~30KB newsletter_html_authoring_spec, so each lesson-authoring Opus call carries the irrelevant newsletter spec and wastes input tokens; a purpose-scoped context load is a future cleanup. **No cron / no RLS beyond lesson_open_responses / no other schema changes; ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched. Edge fn versions: lesson-open-response-feedback v1 NEW, draft-lesson-block v16, scaffold-lesson-outline v27, expand-lesson-from-outline v28; ai-authoring-chat v14 unchanged.** Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v146, this v141 entry, session-140-to-141.md.*

*v138 - Session 136 CLOSE. **AI lesson-builder windowed generation + content-item Pexels ingest; one new edge fn, one edge fn versioned, frontend-only image/batch wiring. No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold).** **EXPAND WINDOWING (durable, expand-lesson-from-outline v24, verify_jwt false).** The full-content generator accepts optional generate_start_index + generate_count. When both are present it renders the ENTIRE approved outline as context (each item tagged "(GENERATE)" or "(context only)") but instructs the model to emit blocks ONLY for the window [start, start+count) and return exactly that many, in order; the audit row + JSON response echo generate_start_index / generate_count / windowed. When the two params are ABSENT the behavior is byte-identical to v13 (whole outline generated in one call) - the change is additive and backward-compatible. Rationale: a single all-blocks call hits the ~150s edge wall-clock and the 8000-output-token cap on long outlines; windowing bounds each call. BATCHING IS CLIENT-DRIVEN (durable): AiPane loops expand per window and accumulates blocks, deliberately NOT server self-chaining (the generate-all-facets EdgeRuntime.waitUntil self-chain is unreliable mid-chain). Full-outline-as-context (not a running prose summary) is the coherence mechanism, chosen over the lighter frontend-slice approach. The shared modules (impersonation_gate, markdown_to_tiptap, length_guidance) and transformConfigForCanvas are unchanged; the image transform still returns asset_id:null and the prompt still forbids the model from sourcing media. **LESSON IMAGE INGEST (durable, lesson-ingest-pexels-asset v1, verify_jwt true, super-admin gated).** Parallel to the newsletter ingest-pexels-asset but for lessons: it rehosts a Pexels image into the private lesson asset pipeline for a content_item (validates item_type='lesson'), calling request_asset_upload(p_content_item_id, p_ref_field='image_asset') then finalize_asset_upload, with an images.pexels.com SSRF allowlist, a HEAD size(<=15MB)/mime guard, a service-role upload, and provenance written to content_asset_versions.generation_provenance. SEARCH reuses newsletter-image-search verbatim (search-only, brand-agnostic; returns candidates with src_large/src_thumb/photographer/photo_page_url/alt) - no new search backend. The Option-B content_item-scoped asset (lesson_block_id NULL) rebinds to the block on save by matching (asset_id, content_item_id, lesson_block_id IS NULL), the existing §60 pattern. **IMAGE ATTRIBUTION (durable).** The lesson image block config carries an optional attribution string set only by the author-facing picker (e.g. "Photo by NAME on Pexels"); the renderer null-coalesces it and the AI generators never emit it, so block-parity (§61) does not require touching the AI edge functions - attribution is a pure frontend-additive field. **AI-BUILDER FLOW (durable).** Outline-stage image items carry image_query / image_resolved{asset_id,attribution,thumb_url} / image_skipped on the persisted outline state; the outline cannot be approved until every image item is resolved or explicitly skipped; on build, each resolved image is stitched (asset_id + attribution) onto its block by global outline index. Stage 3 builds in windows of detailed 5 / standard 7 / concise 10, shows "Sections X of Y built", and gates finalize until all sections are built; the accumulated full_content state persists so a reload resumes mid-build. **Edge fn versions: expand-lesson-from-outline v24 (windowing), lesson-ingest-pexels-asset v1 NEW; no others changed. No cron / RLS / schema changes; ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched.** Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v144, this v138 entry, session-136-to-137.md.*

*v140 - Session 139 CLOSE. **Lesson Experience uplift Phase 1: a render-time per-lesson brand-variable layer (colors + fonts) becomes the home for all lesson-block theming, plus section bands / progress indicators / paced-reveal animation / brand-aware pull-quote, all frontend. No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold; reinforces the §137 React hooks-order convention).** **PER-LESSON BRAND-VARIABLE LAYER (durable, the architectural center of this session).** Before Session 139, only the cover (LessonTitleCard) and the brand editor read lesson_brands; the lesson BLOCKS had no render-time brand layer, and per-block background tints were baked at generation time. Now the trainee viewer (src/components/learning/viewers/LessonBlockViewer.tsx) and the authoring editor (src/pages/super-admin/LessonBlocksEditor.tsx) both query lesson_brands (reusing the lessonBrandQueryKey exported by LessonTitleCard) and set CSS custom properties on their content wrappers via a lessonBrandVars style object: color_primary -> --lesson-primary, color_cta -> --lesson-cta, color_accent -> --lesson-accent, color_surface -> --lesson-surface (each defaulting to the BrainWise hex), plus --font-display and the body fontFamily from the brand font keys. The block stylesheet (lesson-blocks.css) and the block renderer (BlockRenderer.tsx) CONSUME those vars (var(--lesson-*, <default>) in CSS; property-scoped inline var() in the renderer; Tailwind arbitrary values bg-[var(--lesson-cta)] for the tabs) instead of literal brand hexes. The cover continues to self-brand via its own --cover-* inline vars; the wrapper vars theme everything else (bands, blocks, pull-quote, callouts, tabs, flashcards, buttons). DESIGN LOCK (durable): the render-time wrapper-var layer is where new lesson-block colors and fonts must be wired - do NOT reintroduce literal brand hexes into lesson-blocks.css or BlockRenderer.tsx. KEEP-FIXED, never branded (durable): the status/semantic colors forest #2D6A4F (success/correct/done), red #D62828 (error), amber #FFB703 (warning), gray #6D6875 + Tailwind grays (muted), and white; and the readableTextColorForBg WCAG-luminance contrast helper (its #021F36/#FFFFFF returns are literal). The renderer sweep was property-scoped precisely so the contrast helper is never rewritten. Callout info brands to --lesson-accent and important to --lesson-cta via color-mix(in srgb, var(...) 10%, #ffffff); warning/success stay semantic. **BRAND FONTS (durable).** Tailwind's font-display utility maps to a literal Poppins/Montserrat stack (NOT var(--font-display)), and --font-display is undefined globally, so block headings did not follow the brand. Fix: HeadingRender dropped the font-display class for an inline fontFamily: var(--font-display, 'Poppins','Montserrat',system-ui,sans-serif); the viewer/editor wrappers set --font-display (brand display font or the Poppins default) so both the heading inline-var and the block CSS that already reads var(--font-display) follow the brand, and the wrapper body fontFamily makes block body text adopt the brand body font (whole-lesson-body, matching the cover). Assumes the FONT_MAP fonts are loaded app-wide (the same assumption the cover already makes); if a brand picks an unloaded font it falls back. **SHARED EXTRACTIONS (durable).** Two helpers were pulled out of LessonTitleCard so the cover, viewer, and editor share one source: lessonEstimate.ts (BLOCK_MINUTE_WEIGHTS + estimateMinutes, the "~N min" math) and lessonFonts.ts (FONT_MAP + resolveFont). The cover now imports both; its local copies were removed. **SECTION MODEL / VIS-1/2/5/7 (durable rendering facts).** A "section" in the trainee viewer is the run of blocks between button_stack continue delimiters (the delimiter is consumed, not rendered); the scaffold seeds each section with a leading level-2 heading. VIS-1: each section now renders a numbered band (navy-tint + orange left rule + numbered badge + section title + estimateMinutes chip) that REPLACES the section's leading heading, carrying that heading's setBlockRef + data-block-id so the heading-keyed TOC scroll still lands; degrades to number + time when a section has no heading. VIS-2: a section is "complete" when it has been visited AND all its gating-required blocks are in completedIds (lesson_block_progress backed); the TOC shows an orange header progress bar + "X/Y" + per-entry done/active/todo markers. VIS-5: bw-section-enter (lesson-blocks.css, 280ms fade + 8px rise, prefers-reduced-motion guarded) replays on each Continue because the band+blocks wrapper is keyed on the section index. VIS-7: the quote block renders via a .bw-pullquote class (brand-var driven). **HOOKS-ORDER (reinforces §137).** LessonBlockViewer.tsx had its tocEntries + activeTopicId useMemos after the loading/error early returns; the rebuilt 42-block lesson reliably loaded assets first and tripped React #310. Both useMemos were moved above the loading guard. The durable convention stands: every hook precedes every conditional early return. **No edge function / cron / RLS / schema changes this session; ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched.** Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v145, this v140 entry, session-139-to-140.md.*

*v137 - Session 135 CLOSE. **Live-platform bug-fix + dashboard feature-gating; one config function hardened, no schema changes, no new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold).** **ONBOARDING GATE (durable).** has_required_demographics(p_user_id) now requires ONLY the three user-supplied demographic fields (role_in_org, industry, years_experience) for every non-exempt account_type; coach + brainwise_super_admin remain exempt; the onboarding_completed_at non-null short-circuit is preserved. department_id and org_level NO LONGER gate onboarding completion - they are invite/admin-assigned, legitimately null for a brand-new org with no departments or an unassigned invite, and previously made the gate unsatisfiable, producing an infinite ProtectedRoute redirect to /demographic-form. *v136 - Session 134 CLOSE. **Operations/CRM externalization-track: per-org Operations invoice-email branding + CRM/Operations workspace-access provisioning, both backend-first and verified; plus the durable lesson-assets storage-access rationale. No new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold).** **PER-ORG INVOICE-EMAIL BRANDING (durable).** operations.organizations gained sender_display_name, reply_to_email, email_logo_enabled (boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false). RPC ops_get_org_email_branding(p_org) (SECDEF, service_role only) returns the email-branding bundle (name, sender_display_name, reply_to_email, legal_name, logo_url, brand_color, accent_color, email_logo_enabled) plus stripe_collection_enabled. ops_update_org_branding(p_patch jsonb) extended (same signature) to accept the three new fields. ops_get_public_document_by_token invoice branch also returns collects_payment = COALESCE(org.stripe_collection_enabled,false). Edge fn ops-invoice-send v14 reads org branding and renders: From DISPLAY NAME = COALESCE(sender_display_name,name,'BrainWise'), brand/accent colors from the org, footer name = COALESCE(legal_name,name), logo only when email_logo_enabled, reply_to only when set, CTA label 'View & Pay Invoice' when the org collects payment else 'View Invoice'. RESEND CONSTRAINT (durable): Resend can only send from a DNS-verified domain, so there is ONE shared sending mailbox (invoices@mail.brainwiseenterprises.com) for all orgs and per-tenant identity is expressed only through the From display name + reply_to + body branding, never a per-tenant From address. STRIPE COLLECTION (durable): there is one STRIPE_SECRET_KEY (BrainWise's) and no Stripe Connect, so all Operations invoice payments settle to BrainWise; only BrainWise has stripe_collection_enabled=true; ops-public-invoice-checkout gates on ops_stripe_collection_enabled(org) (403 when disabled) and every Stripe object carries ops_org_id metadata, so per-tenant Connect can be added later without reshaping the data. Deferred externalization-branding: per-org custom From-domain and the /pay/:token public page header literal. **CRM/OPERATIONS WORKSPACE-ACCESS PROVISIONING (durable).** A user's access to the CRM/Operations workspace is an active row in operations.users (id = auth uid; org_id, email, full_name, role operations.user_role admin|sales_manager|sales_user|read_only, status, manager_id) - this is SEPARATE from the module nav, which is gated by user_has_feature('module:CRM'/'module:OPERATIONS'). The platform org links to its ops workspace via operations.organizations.platform_org_id (nullable uuid; partial unique index organizations_platform_org_id_key WHERE platform_org_id IS NOT NULL; plain uuid, NO cross-schema FK per Doc-5 Rule 1). ops_provision_customer_org (6-arg, p_platform_org_id uuid DEFAULT NULL) AUTO-DERIVES platform_org_id from the provisioning admin's public.users.organization_id when not supplied, but ONLY for org_admin/company_admin admins (coach/individual user-mode workspaces stay unlinked). Four access RPCs (SECDEF, REVOKE PUBLIC,anon + GRANT authenticated,service_role): ops_grant_operations_access(p_user_id, p_role, p_platform_org_id DEFAULT NULL) takes a super-admin path (resolve the ops org via platform_org_id after assert_super_admin) or an org-admin path (operations.current_org_id() + current_user_role()='admin'), upserts ON CONFLICT(id); ops_revoke_operations_access(p_user_id, p_platform_org_id DEFAULT NULL) sets status='inactive'; ops_org_user_admin_list(p_platform_org_id) is the super-admin read; ops_org_user_list() is the org-admin read. GUARD (durable): the workspace can never be left with zero active admins - grant refuses to demote the only active admin to a lesser role, and revoke refuses to deactivate the last active admin. Existing org-mode ops workspaces created before platform_org_id were backfilled from their admin's platform org (org/company admins only), so a super-admin or coach workspace whose admin has no corporate platform org stays unlinked by design. ENTITLEMENT (re-confirmed, durable): module:CRM and module:OPERATIONS resolve INDEPENDENTLY through principal_has_module -> module_entitlements with module_definitions defaults (both default-off); an ops seat (operations.users row) is orthogonal to the module entitlement, and the sidebar adds the CRM and Operations navs independently per module. **LESSON-ASSETS STORAGE ACCESS (durable rationale; do not regress).** The private lesson-assets bucket intentionally has NO trainee storage SELECT policy. Trainee delivery is RPC-gated signing: useLessonBlockAssets -> edge fn get-lesson-block-asset-urls (v11, verify_jwt false, JWT-in-body) -> RPC get_lesson_block_assets_for_trainee (SECDEF), which enforces LMS module entitlement + self/super-admin/mentor + the content_item being a published non-archived lesson + an active/completed user_curriculum_assignments row on a curriculum whose curriculum_modules contains the parent module, THEN a service_role client signs each object (2h expiry). This is the single authorization checkpoint and the SCORM/export seam (viewers must never call supabase.storage directly). A trainee storage SELECT policy must NOT be added: it is redundant (signed-URL fetches are validated by the storage signing key, not RLS), it would open a direct authenticated read/enumerate path that bypasses the RPC checkpoint, and the private bucket exposes no guessable URLs. A Lovable storage scanner will keep flagging the absence of the policy; mark it Ignored with this rationale. **Edge fn versions: ops-invoice-send v14; no others changed. No cron / RLS-on-existing-public-tables / schema changes outside the operations.* columns and RPCs above; ops-stripe-webhook / platform stripe-webhook never touched.** Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v142, this v136 entry, session-134-to-135.md.*

*v135 - Session 133 CLOSE (module-entitlement build; continues the v134 white-label/scoping half of Session 133). **Module Entitlement layer ("Modularize and Sell") Phase 1 built + verified; no new numbered standing rule (§1-§158 hold).** Per-principal on/off for sellable modules (ASSESSMENTS, LMS, CRM, OPERATIONS) across corporate orgs, individuals, and coaches, resolved by one function; orthogonal to the 5.3 tenant-isolation model. **TABLES (public).** module_definitions(module PK, label, default_enabled, is_sellable, is_enforced); seeds LMS + ASSESSMENTS default_enabled=true/is_enforced=true, CRM + OPERATIONS default_enabled=false/is_enforced=false, all is_sellable=true; is_enforced = "this layer actually controls access for the module today." module_entitlements(id, principal_type CHECK(user|org), user_id XOR org_id [FK users/organizations ON DELETE CASCADE, XOR CHECK], module FK, source, source_ref, granted_by, starts_at, ends_at, revoked_at, effect CHECK(grant|deny), created_at, updated_at); indexes uq_module_ent_source_ref UNIQUE(source,source_ref,module) WHERE source_ref IS NOT NULL (purchase/webhook idempotency), uq_module_ent_active_user / uq_module_ent_active_org partial-unique per principal+module WHERE revoked_at IS NULL. module_subscription_prices(stripe_price_id PK, module FK, grant_kind default 'subscription'); empty, subscription-readiness only. **RLS.** module_definitions SELECT to authenticated, writes service_role/migration only; module_entitlements SELECT-own (user_id=auth.uid() OR org_id=current_user_org_id()), no client writes, service_role full; module_subscription_prices service_role only. **RESOLVER + SEAM.** principal_has_module(p_user,p_module) (SECDEF STABLE, service_role-only EXEC): super-admin -> true; most-specific active explicit override wins (user-level grant/deny beats org-level grant/deny; active = revoked_at IS NULL AND starts_at<=now() AND (ends_at IS NULL OR ends_at>now())); else module_definitions.default_enabled; else false. user_has_feature intercepts feature LIKE 'module:%' at the top -> principal_has_module(user, module-name); all prior non-module behavior preserved; single seam inherited by SubscriptionGate and any RPC/RLS. **WRITE PATH / RPCs.** _module_entitlement_upsert(principal_type,user_id,org_id,module,source,source_ref,granted_by,ends_at,effect) (SECDEF, service_role-only): idempotent on (source,source_ref,module) when source_ref set, else upserts the single active principal+module row flipping effect. module_entitlement_grant / module_entitlement_deny / module_entitlement_revoke (super-admin; EXEC authenticated+service_role): each asserts assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows('permission_change'), requires reason>=10, audits via log_super_admin_action; grant->effect grant (default source manual_invoice), deny->effect deny (source manual_deny), revoke->sets revoked_at (clears to module default). module_entitlement_admin_list(principal_type,user_id,org_id) (SECDEF, super-admin): per sellable module returns default_enabled, is_enforced, override_effect, override_source, override_ends_at, effective_enabled; powers the admin toggles. assert_module_entitled(p_module): reusable backend deny primitive; raises authentication_required or module_not_entitled (ERRCODE 42501). **AUDIT.** Action types module_entitlement_grant / _deny / _revoke registered in super_admin_action_types (category user_management, requires_justification, is_mutation, denylist_during_impersonation). NOTE (durable): super_admin_audit_log.action_type FK-references super_admin_action_types, so any new logged action type MUST be registered first or the logging RPC fails. **ENFORCEMENT POINTS.** Backend LMS, caller=consumer: get_content_item_video_playback, get_resource_content_asset, self_enroll_in_module, self_enroll_in_curriculum, self_enroll_in_certification_path. Backend LMS, on-behalf-capable (gate on the target learner via principal_has_module(v_target_id,'LMS')): get_content_item_video_asset, get_lesson_block_assets_for_trainee. Backend ASSESSMENTS (coarse switch above the per-instrument entitlements; instruments unchanged): start_assessment (jsonb error module_not_entitled), start_epn_assessment (raise) - begin-chokepoint only, in-progress + results untouched. Frontend: SubscriptionGate routes module:* through user_has_feature for every principal before the bypass shortcut (coaches gateable, super-admins pass via the resolver); gated routes = 7 learner LMS (module:LMS: /resources, /my-learning, /resources/:resourceId, /learning/cert-path/:certPathId, /learning/curriculum/:curriculumId, /learning/module/:moduleId, /learning/content-item/:contentItemId) + 3 ASSESSMENTS take-routes (/assessment, /epn-complete/:assignmentId, /airsa-manager-complete/:managerAssessmentId). Admin: ModuleEntitlementsPanel on CompanyDetail "Modules" tab (org) + the member Access tab (individuals + coaches). **ENFORCED / DEFAULT MATRIX.** LMS default-on, enforced; ASSESSMENTS default-on, enforced; CRM default-off, not enforced; OPERATIONS default-off, not enforced. **DEFERRED.** assert_module_entitled('LMS') built + tested but not wired onto learner RPCs (no-op while LMS default-on; attach when flipped to gated, at get_module_detail + learner content/resource entry RPCs + signed-URL edge functions get-content-item-video-url / get-resource-signed-url). *v133 - Sessions 131 + 132 CLOSE (one continuous edge-function remediation arc). **Platform-wide "Conflicting API keys" edge-function bug found and fully eradicated; no feature or Operations work.** One new standing rule (§158); §1-§157 hold. **§158 NEW: edge-to-edge fetch must use MATCHED API keys.** A recent Supabase gateway change rejects any fetch from one edge function to another /functions/v1/ function whose `apikey` and `Authorization` headers carry two DIFFERENT Supabase keys (anon in one, service-role in the other) with a 401 "Conflicting API keys" returned BEFORE the target function executes. RULE: any edge function that fetches another edge function must send the SAME key in both headers (anon in both is the canonical safe shape). THREE IMMUNE PATTERNS (no change needed): (1) supabase.functions.invoke(), the client sends matched keys automatically; (2) Resend-direct sends (https://api.resend.com), no Supabase key pair at all; (3) fetches carrying ONLY x-internal-secret with no apikey/Authorization pair. ALSO SAFE: a user-JWT in Authorization paired with apikey:anon, because a user JWT is not a Supabase API key, so there is no anon-vs-service conflict, this is the normal authenticated-request shape (generate-report and ai-chat both call check-ai-usage this way; the whole AI generator family is safe by this route). service+service matched keys also pass (submit-contact-request / submit-briefing-request call send-email this way). DIAGNOSIS SIGNATURE: an invoking function logs a 200 while the callee logs a 401 with a null function_id and ~0ms duration (the gateway rejected it before dispatch); the caller's catch then drives a degraded fallback (here, an "email_sent:false" path that surfaced a manual invite code). The fix is purely the header keys, send-email's own auth is unaffected (it authenticates callers via x-internal-secret, not the bearer), so lowering the bearer to anon changes no authorization. **THE BUG THIS SURFACED.** invitation_send / bulk_invitation_send (and a family of sibling functions) fetched send-email with apikey=ANON + Authorization=Bearer SERVICE_ROLE, so every invite email died at the gateway and the super-admin/org invite UI fell back to a manual code. The frontend (CompanyMembersSection, CompanyInvitationsSection) was correct (it only shows the manual code on email_sent:false), not a frontend bug. **15 FUNCTIONS FIXED** (lowered the send-email / send-departure-emails fetch's Authorization from service-role to anon to match apikey; all boot-verified). Session 131 (14): invitation_send v23, bulk_invitation_send v21, assign_epn_send, airsa-supervisor-invite, invite-coach, coach_invitation_resend, airsa-supervisor-reminder, deactivate-and-notify, bulk-deactivate-and-notify, dispatch-grace-reminders, verify-conversion, generate-departure-export, admin_trigger_password_reset, bulk_coach_invite. Session 132 (1): stripe-webhook v41, the idiom lived ONLY in the sendInvitationEmail helper's fetch to send-email, firing on the coach_order / coach_bulk_order branches inside try/catch; it does NOT touch signature verification, DB writes, coupon recalc, or subscription tiering. Authorization lowered to SUPABASE_ANON_KEY, redeployed verify_jwt false, boot-verified (no-signature POST returns HTTP 400 "Missing signature or webhook secret"). Held in Session 131 pending Cole's explicit greenlight (standing discipline: never touch the platform stripe-webhook by reflex; ops-stripe-webhook id be435d9f and platform stripe-webhook id fb9725d2 are never cross-modified), greenlit and fixed in Session 132. INTERIM-DEPLOY NOTE: a deploy briefly pushed a PLACEHOLDER stub as v40 for ~90s; Stripe auto-retries non-2xx webhooks so no events were lost, and v41 restored the full corrected source immediately. **FULL SWEEP (Session 132), all ~95 edge functions reconciled; every function outside the 15 is CLEAN.** Email senders are either fixed or already safe (ops sender/cron family + newsletter-dispatch are Resend-direct; send-departure-emails / crm-email-send / crm-email-inbound are Resend-direct; submit-contact-request / submit-briefing-request use matched service+service keys). Every edge-to-edge orchestration call elsewhere uses functions.invoke, x-internal-secret-only fetches, or the safe user-JWT+anon shape. Storage/mux/asset, impersonation, check-*/log-audit, newsletter read-only, both Stripe webhooks, and the diagnostics carry no edge-to-edge send-email call at all. The discriminator is now unambiguous, so the sweep is exhaustive and should not be re-run. **NO schema / RLS / cron / table changes, edge-function source only.** diag-internal-secret-check and diag-resend-harness neutered to inert 410 stubs (Cole to delete from the dashboard; MCP has no delete-function). Most org-admin write RPCs carry a gate-read `IF current_user_account_type()='brainwise_super_admin' THEN <skip org check>` branch (invitation_create, bulk_invitation_create, department_create/rename/delete, user_assign_supervisor, user_deactivate/reactivate, member_feature_override_set, reconcile_supervisors_for_org, admin_promote_to_org_admin), and users/corporate_invitations/departments/organizations each have a brainwise_super_admin SELECT-all policy, so cross-org reads (incl. admin_org_users_view, verified 59 rows for the test org under a JWT-sim'd authenticated role) and most writes already worked. admin_org_users_view authoritative columns: id, email, full_name, account_type, organization_id, department_id, org_level, deactivated_at, reactivation_deadline, deactivation_reason, supervisor_user_id, department_joined_id, department_joined_name, supervisor_joined_id/email/full_name. **NEW/CHANGED BACKEND (4).** (1) public.admin_assign_or_invite_org_admin(p_organization_id uuid, p_email text) RETURNS jsonb — SECDEF, search_path public, assert_super_admin, REVOKE PUBLIC/anon + GRANT authenticated/service_role. (2) supervisor_dashboard_set — added a brainwise_super_admin cross-org branch (previously org-admin-own-org only and explicitly blocked super admins); company_admin still excluded; audit row actor_role brainwise_super_admin in company_admin_audit_log. (3) invitation_send EDGE FN v22 (id e5d7f6b4-3554-4f4a-a202-7ac3109122b3, verify_jwt false, owns the branded invite email via send-email): the v21 hard requirement of super_admin_session_id for super admins (impersonation-era) was REMOVED; routing is now `useSessionAdminPath = isSuperAdmin && !!body.super_admin_session_id` -> session-bearing super admin uses admin_invitation_create (impersonation path preserved), everyone else (org/company admin AND session-LESS super admin) uses invitation_create (its super-admin cross-org branch). This is the single change that lets a NON-impersonation super admin send real invite emails (org-admin via account_type:'org_admin', general member single via this fn, bulk via bulk_invitation_send -> bulk_invitation_create). account_type passes through. (4) public.admin_invitation_revoke(p_invitation_id uuid) RETURNS jsonb — SECDEF super-admin-only; hard-DELETEs a pending (redeemed_at IS NULL) corporate_invitations row + super_admin_audit_log 'invitation_revoked'; raises 22023 on not-found or already-redeemed. NOTE: corporate_invitations has SELECT policies only (no UPDATE/DELETE), so revoke MUST be a SECDEF RPC; and a redeemed_consistency CHECK requires redeemed_at + redeemed_by_user_id to be set together. super_admin_audit_log.action_type is an FK to super_admin_action_types (a lookup table, NOT a CHECK); two rows registered this session: 'org_admin_invited' (now unused/harmless) and 'invitation_revoked' (settings cloned from corporate_invitation_created). department_delete(p_dept_id, p_action, p_reassign_to_dept_id) accepts p_action 'reassign' (same-org non-self destination, moves users.department_id) or 'unassign' (null destination, sets users.department_id NULL) ONLY, then deletes the dept; department_rename enforces non-empty/<=100 chars/unique-within-org (23505). **FRONTEND COMPONENTS (4 new + edits, all SHA-verified).** src/components/super-admin/CompanyMembersSection.tsx (b153331c, Members tab: org-admin card + roster per-row supervisor/deactivate/reactivate + reconcile + supervisor-dashboard toggle), CompanyInvitationsSection.tsx (bda31965, Invitations tab: single + bulk[mirrors AdminUsers, XLSX, 75 cap, bulk_invitation_send] + pending list + revoke), CompanyDepartmentsSection.tsx (ee4fb53a, Departments tab: create/rename/delete-with-reassign), all wired into CompanyDetail.tsx (68aaeb9b). Frontend-only, SHA-verified. Coach-dashboard additions shipped alongside. **SESSION-TAIL READOUTS (no code shipped; recorded as durable architecture facts).** (A) **+10 AI-chat grant (item 2) is scaffolded but UNWIRED.** The one-time +10 chat grant exists in the DB as an idempotent, correct grant function, but `check-ai-usage` does NOT honor `one_time_chat_credits`, so the +10 is currently inert for every path and all 17 coaches receive no AI chat at all. Extending it is therefore not "a couple of grant calls", it is wiring an unconnected mechanism, and all the work lives in Edge Functions (`check-ai-usage` plus the purchase / comp / invite webhooks). Open design decisions before any build: (1) does +10 stack on the monthly tier allowance or is it the sole allowance for otherwise-denied users (comped clients, coaches); (2) where each grant fires, especially the super-admin comp/invite path that has no Stripe checkout event to hang on; (3) the `source_ref` idempotency key per path. Cole's Session-129 decision: fix enforcement for regular per-assessment purchasers FIRST (Phase A), then extend to coach-paid + super-admin-invited (Phase B). (B) **White-label readiness (item 5) is greenfield.** Schema-wide scan: ZERO branding/logo/theme/color/favicon/custom-CSS/subdomain/custom-domain columns anywhere; `organizations` carries only operational columns (name, status, seat_count, admin_user_id, primary_contact_email, mfa_required, is_internal_test). Tenancy is uneven: the operations/CRM schema is org-partitioned on ~100 tables/views, but the core public schema (users, assessments, learning) is largely NOT org_id-partitioned (org affiliation runs through `organizations.admin_user_id` + seat/membership relationships, so there is no uniform tenant key and no per-session "which org's brand applies" resolver). No custom-domain or subdomain routing (single domain). Theming is global (brand tokens are app-level CSS variables, not org-driven). A white-label product surface is a net-new multi-session capability, not a config toggle; realistic ordering is branding-layer-on-organizations + session-time CSS-variable injection first, the org-brand resolver next, tenant-isolation hardening for the non-partitioned public schema, then custom domains last. Cole's Session-129 decision: build the full track ("all of it"). (C) **Lesson-block editor location (item 12).** `LessonBlocksEditor` lives at `/super-admin/content-authoring/lessons/:contentItemId` and is reachable only by opening a saved `lesson_blocks` content item in the content-item editor and clicking "Edit lesson blocks"; because blocks are keyed to a `content_item_id`, the editor cannot be fully decoupled from a content item, so "surfacing" means adding a more direct entry point (small/frontend). Cole's Session-129 decision: Option B, but the recovered transcript ended before the A/B/C entry-point options were written out, so the Session-129 opener must restate the options before building. **Edge fn versions: none changed. *v129 - Session 127 CLOSE. **BrainWise SaaS platform session: Item 2a (PTP report persistent highlighting) built end-to-end and verified, backend + frontend; assessment slider/navigation fixes; a security-scan remediation + triage pass; no Operations work.** No new numbered standing rule (the existing set holds; this session reinforces §156/§157 grant discipline, the §92 repo↔runtime sync, and adds an operational practice on the Lovable security scanner, recorded below). SCHEMA (public schema, 1 table).** public.ptp_report_highlights (id uuid PK; viewer_user_id uuid FK users CASCADE = the reader who made the highlight; assessment_result_id uuid FK assessment_results CASCADE; context_tab text NOT NULL CHECK in (professional, personal, combined, single); block_key text = the per-section anchor key; start_offset int CHECK >=0; end_offset int; CONSTRAINT prh_offsets_valid CHECK end_offset>start_offset; block_text_sha text = a cyrb53 hash of the anchored block text at creation; quoted_text text = the exact selected substring, used for heal-on-mismatch; color text NULL = palette key; note text NULL = reserved for the future highlight-comment feature [see build-queue v135 item 9]; created_at/updated_at). Index idx_prh_viewer_result_tab on (viewer_user_id, assessment_result_id, context_tab). updated_at via trigger trg_prh_set_updated_at calling prh_set_updated_at() (SECURITY INVOKER, search_path '', REVOKE EXECUTE FROM PUBLIC, anon, authenticated; it fires only as the trigger). **RLS (5 policies).** viewer SELECT/UPDATE/DELETE own (viewer_user_id=auth.uid()); viewer INSERT WITH CHECK (viewer_user_id=auth.uid() AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM assessment_results ar WHERE ar.id=assessment_result_id AND ar.instrument_id='INST-001')); service_role ALL. **KEY DESIGN: the cross-table EXISTS in the INSERT policy is itself RLS-filtered for the authenticated role, so a highlight can only be created against a PTP result the caller can already SELECT** (own, super-admin, coach via coach_clients, direct-share via the v128 disjuncts, org-peer). It rides the existing assessment_results visibility surface instead of re-deriving who-can-see-whom, so it auto-tracks any future change to that surface and duplicates zero visibility logic. No SECDEF write RPCs: the frontend does direct supabase.from('ptp_report_highlights') reads/writes under RLS. Functional RLS test PASSED (rolled-back DO, JWT-sim): owner insert INSERTED, stranger insert BLOCKED 42501, coach (active coach_clients link to the owner) insert INSERTED, owner_sees=1 / coach_sees=1 / stranger_sees=0; zero residue; NOTIFY pgrst run. **PALETTE (locked, Cole-approved, teal default).** Stored as a color key string, rendered to rgba at paint time: teal rgba(0,109,119,0.22) [default], amber rgba(255,183,3,0.38), purple rgba(60,9,108,0.18). Green is deliberately excluded (the green+teal pastel-pairing rule, 5.x). **FRONTEND (3 new files + edits, all SHA-verified).** src/lib/reportHighlightColors.ts: HighlightColor type, HIGHLIGHT_COLORS [teal, amber, purple], DEFAULT_HIGHLIGHT_COLOR='teal', highlightCss(key), blockTextSha(text) = a synchronous cyrb53 hash (chosen over async SubtleCrypto so anchoring is synchronous at render). src/hooks/useReportHighlights.ts: loads by assessment_result_id + context_tab grouped byBlock; addHighlight (supabase.auth.getUser then insert), removeHighlight, reload. src/components/results/ReportHighlight.tsx: ReportHighlightProvider (context) + HighlightableText (the wrapper applied to each highlightable block). ANCHORING MODEL: every hook runs before any early return (rules-of-hooks); on render, if the stored block_text_sha matches the current block hash it paints by [start_offset, end_offset]; on a mismatch it heals by indexOf(quoted_text); if neither resolves it drops the stale highlight. Selection capture is single-block only: onMouseUp computes offsets via Range.selectNodeContents + toString().length; the create popover is three color dots, clicking an existing mark opens a Remove popover; popovers are position:fixed. **BLOCK-KEY SCHEME (wired into every PTP report block in src/components/results/PTPNarrativeSections.tsx):** profile_overview, dimension_highlights:{dimId}, cross_assessment, personal_summary:{i}, action_plan:{i}:title | :rationale | :step:{j}, facet_{elevated|suppressed}:{facetName}:{positive_self|negative_self|positive_others|negative_others}:{i}, response:{itemNumber} (the question text), and response:{itemNumber}:{positive_self|...}:{i} (the expanded per-response impact bullets). **GATING (allowHighlighting prop).** MyResults.tsx gained allowHighlighting?: boolean (default true) and wraps PTPNarrativeProvider in ReportHighlightProvider with assessmentResultId + contextTab + enabled. Highlighting stays ON for the owner's own report and the coach client view (ClientResults.tsx). It is forced OFF (allowHighlighting={false}) on every read-only third-party surface: SharedWithMe.tsx, SharedResults.tsx (org-peer), and the super-admin CoachReport.tsx. An explicit prop was required rather than reusing isCoachView: per v128, isCoachView is a shared third-party-viewer flag used by BOTH the coach client view (highlighting should be ON) and the share surfaces (highlighting should be OFF), so it cannot itself gate highlighting. **RESPONSES-ROW SELECTABILITY FIX.** The Assessment Responses question text sat inside a native button (onClick=toggleRow), and native buttons suppress text selection, so a highlight could not start there. Fix: that one row's button was converted to a div with role="button" tabIndex={0} onKeyDown (Enter/Space) and cursor:pointer (only that control changed). Two of Lovable's self-reported "verified fixed" claims were WRONG this session (it reported has_column_privilege=false when it was true), so for any RLS/grant change, trust a live pg introspection check, NOT Lovable's report or migration success. *v128 - Session 126 CLOSE. **BrainWise SaaS platform session: Item 2c (share PTP results by email) built end-to-end, backend + frontend, verified; Item 2a (PTP report persistent highlighting) deferred to Session 127; no Operations work.** No new standing rule (§1 to §157 hold; this session reinforces §156/§157 grant discipline and §92 repo↔runtime sync). Backend-first; every apply_migration followed by a separate execute_sql verification; functional tests single rolled-back DO blocks (sentinel RAISE, zero residue; the raw-RLS test used set_config request.jwt.claims + SET LOCAL ROLE authenticated to force RLS, the SECDEF-RPC test used set_config only). **DIRECTED PTP SHARING MODEL (account-to-account, NOT a tokenized link).** A logged-in owner shares their entire PTP with another existing account-holder by email; the recipient reads the owner's FULL PTP report from a new "Shared With Me" surface and can combine it with their own results in the AI chat. Cross-organization (any account-holder to any other), distinct from the org-bounded peer /shared-results path. **SCHEMA (public schema).** public.ptp_result_shares (id; owner_user_id FK users CASCADE; viewer_user_id FK users CASCADE; created_at; revoked_at NULL = soft-revoke, a revoked row is retained as an audit trail; CHECK owner<>viewer; partial UNIQUE uq_prs_active on (owner_user_id, viewer_user_id) WHERE revoked_at IS NULL = at most one active grant per ordered pair; idx_prs_viewer_active, idx_prs_owner). RLS: owner FOR ALL TO authenticated (owner_user_id=auth.uid()), viewer FOR SELECT TO authenticated (viewer_user_id=auth.uid()), service_role FOR ALL. public.ptp_share_attempts (internal rate-limit / enumeration log; service_role-only RLS + REVOKE ALL FROM authenticated,anon per §157). **RLS HELPER + DISJUNCTS (the access mechanism).** public.direct_ptp_share_visible(p_owner_user_id, p_viewer_user_id) RETURNS boolean SQL STABLE SECDEF search_path='' (true when an active ptp_result_shares row exists AND neither user is deactivated). It is RLS-facing, so it KEEPS the authenticated EXECUTE grant (REVOKE PUBLIC/anon, GRANT authenticated+service_role) — same posture as dp_coach_can_view (v127) and operations.crm_can_write (v125). Four additive SELECT disjuncts were added (no existing policy modified) so a viewer can read the owner's PTP rows: on assessment_results (owner_user_id=user_id), assessments (user_id), assessment_responses (via assessment_id→assessments.user_id), facet_interpretations (via assessment_result_id→assessment_results.user_id) — every disjunct INST-001-scoped, user_id<>auth.uid(), routed through the helper. So a directly-shared PTP is readable through the exact same RLS surface the owner sees, scoped to PTP only; NAI/AIRSA/HSS rows are NOT shared (no disjunct exists for them). **RPCs (4, SECDEF plpgsql, search_path '', REVOKE PUBLIC/anon, GRANT authenticated+service_role).** share_ptp_results(p_target_email text)→jsonb: auth check; a rate-limit guard (≥10 attempts/min raises 'rate_limited' SQLSTATE 53400) logged via ptp_share_attempts; resolves the lower/trim active email; returns {found:false} when no account exists, {found:true,status:self} for the caller's own email, {found:true,status:already_shared,viewer_name} when an active grant exists, else inserts the share + notify_user(viewer,'ptp_results_shared',payload, dedup_key 'ptp_results_shared:'||share_id) + returns {found:true,status:shared,viewer_name}. revoke_ptp_share(p_viewer_user_id uuid)→{revoked} (soft-set revoked_at). list_my_ptp_shares()→{shares:[…]} and list_ptp_shared_with_me()→{shared_with_me:[{share_id,owner_user_id,owner_name,shared_at}]} drive the two UI surfaces. The yes/no email-existence check is an accepted SOC 2 tradeoff: the enumeration vector is authenticated, attributable, and membership-only, backstopped by the rate-limit + the ptp_share_attempts audit log. **NOTIFICATION.** notification_types_catalog row 'ptp_results_shared' (category 'sharing', channel in_app, user_configurable true, is_v1_active true); notification_display gained a 'ptp_results_shared' case (preserves all prior cases; deep-link COALESCE(action_url, /shared-with-me)). Per the v127 catalog-driven fact, this type auto-surfaces in NotificationSettings and is email-capable via compose_notification_email with no extra frontend work. **AI-CHAT COMBINE (ai-chat Edge Function, id de20b993-2ff5-471f-9656-1d10c34854fc, v50, verify_jwt FALSE).** The deployed v49 read only the caller's own assessment_result_ids (hard-filtered to user_id=caller) and ignored peer_result_ids entirely. v50 adds a shared-results path: it fetches peer_result_ids via the caller's RLS-scoped user client (so access is enforced by the four disjuncts, not by trust — arbitrary ids return nothing), filters out the caller's own ids, labels each block "Shared by {name}", adds a framing note, and caps total model context at MAX_CONTEXT_RESULTS=12; the own-results path (service role + user_id filter) is unchanged. **isCoachView IS A THIRD-PARTY-VIEWER FLAG, NOT A COACH-RELATIONSHIP GATE (durable architecture fact, verified this session by reading both files).** MyResults.tsx + PTPNarrativeSections.tsx render another user's PTP read-only via isCoachView=true + targetUserId + viewLabel (the same prop combo the org-peer SharedResults page uses). On the PTP report, isCoachView has exactly two effects: (a) isCoachLimited = isCoachView && permissionLevel==='score_summary' (so with full_results or undefined it never fires and the full report renders) and (b) it hides the "Add to my Development Plan" button (correct: a viewer must not add the owner's actions to their own plan). The coach_clients filter is guarded by coachUserId (not passed on a share view, so no coach lookups run) and the NAI coach toggle is unreachable (a share viewer can only RLS-read PTP). No coach-specific content is injected. permissionLevel and defaultInstrumentId are inert on a share view (only PTP is RLS-readable, so the instrument selector lands on PTP regardless, and permissionLevel only matters through the score_summary gate). Optional future cleanup: rename isCoachView to a sharedView prop for clarity (no behavior change; declined for 2c). **FRONTEND (3 cycles, all SHA-verified).** PrivacySettings.tsx gained a "Share My PTP Results" card (hasPtp-gated; share_ptp_results / list_my_ptp_shares / revoke_ptp_share). NEW shared helper operations.crm_can_write(p_owner uuid) (STABLE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path ''): returns true when current_user_role()='admin' (any owner), or owner=auth.uid() (sales_user, and a manager's own), or current_user_role()='sales_manager' AND owner IN (SELECT id FROM operations.users WHERE manager_id=auth.uid()); read_only and any other role return false; the whole result is COALESCEd to false, so a null owner is not-writable for non-admins. The helper is REVOKEd FROM PUBLIC and GRANTed to authenticated+service_role (it must be EXECUTE-able by the role evaluating the policy, so it is deliberately NOT §156-locked off authenticated; it accepts only an owner uuid and derives everything from the caller's own identity, so it leaks nothing and has no forge surface). DESIGN FACT: operations.users.id = auth.uid() on this project, so write-own is simply owner_user_id=auth.uid() with no users lookup. The RLS on the five owner-bearing CRM tables (leads, accounts, contact_persons, deals, activities) was rewritten: SELECT unchanged (org_id=current_org_id() only, so every role reads all in-org, which is why the dashboard and the report_crm_* security_invoker views are unaffected by Phase 10); INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE now require org_id=current_org_id() AND operations.crm_can_write(owner_user_id) (UPDATE carries it in both USING and WITH CHECK, so a non-admin cannot reassign a row out of their own scope). Per-table role targeting preserved (leads/accounts/deals/activities TO public, contact_persons TO authenticated; anon is blocked at the table-grant layer regardless). Child/junction and config tables (deal_line_items, deal_stage_history, deal_team_members, deal_stakeholders, activity_attendees/attachments, campaigns, campaign_attribution, lead_scoring_rules, workflow_rules) keep org-scoped writes (no owner column; a user who can see the parent edits its sub-rows). DELETE moved from admin-only to owner-based (write-own includes delete-own per §5.14). All SECDEF RPCs (ops_convert_lead, the Won bridge, the scoring engine) and the attribution triggers run as owner and bypass RLS, so conversion/webhook/scoring paths are unaffected. Verified by a rolled-back JWT-sim role matrix on leads (all five roles) and again on accounts/contacts/deals/activities; synthetic auth.users rows were seeded inside the transaction under session_replication_role=replica to skip the on_auth_user_created sync triggers, then operations.users + fixtures, all rolled back via a sentinel RAISE with zero residue.
