*v124 - Session 122 CLOSE. **Operations Doc-2 CRM Phases 7 (lead scoring + assignment + workflow engine) and 8 (campaigns, attribution, reports, dashboard, settings UI) COMPLETE and verified (backend + frontend).** No new standing rule (§1-§157 hold; this session reinforces §156 and adds the org_id-default convention below). Backend-first; every apply_migration followed by a separate execute_sql verification; every functional test a single rolled-back DO block (sentinel RAISE, zero residue); frontend verified by GitHub API SHA (raw CDN can be stale, per §117). **PHASE 7: LEAD SCORING + ASSIGNMENT + WORKFLOW ENGINE.** lead_scoring_rules (rule_type CHECK demographic|behavioral|decay) + append-only lead_score_events (the score audit trail); scoring engine operations._recompute_lead_score(lead) (internal) + public ops_recompute_lead_score (authenticated, manual recompute from the lead detail ScoreCard); score-decay cron jobid 31; round-robin owner assignment. workflow_rules + workflow_execution_log (dedup so a rule fires once per target). The workflow engine is SCAN-BASED, not trigger-based: operations.ops_workflow_engine_run scans for due conditions on each cron tick (jobid 32, '3-59/5 * * * *') and handles 4 kinds: won_to_customer / deal_stale / lead_qualified_assign / deal_discovery_task. DESIGN RATIONALE (locked): a scan-based engine avoids the recursion and re-entrancy hazards of per-row table triggers on deals/leads (a stage change firing a rule that mutates the deal that re-fires the trigger); the Won bridge runs here as an ADDITIVE internal helper operations._won_bridge_create_customer invoked by the won_to_customer scan rather than as an on-Won trigger, mirroring the same additive-helper choice used for the Phase-1 ops_create_customer_from_deal (an org-guarded RPC cannot be called from the service-role scan path because it would raise; the additive internal helper derives context from the row and never raises). 4 seeded workflow rules. Frontend (verified by API SHA): ScoreCard on OperationsLeadDetail (recompute via ops_recompute_lead_score + score-event history from lead_score_events); LeadScoringRulesCard (full CRUD, dialog fields conditional on rule_type: demographic/behavioral build a trigger_condition, decay forces score_adjustment 0; buildTriggerCondition maps 'in' to an array and is_null/is_not_null omit the value) + WorkflowRulesCard (edit-only over the seeded rules, active toggle, per-kind params delay_minutes/stale_days/stage_name preserving trigger_config.kind) in a NEW 'CRM Automation' tab on OperationsSettings (all existing tabs unchanged). **PHASE 8: CAMPAIGNS + ATTRIBUTION + REPORTS + DASHBOARD.** campaigns + campaign_attribution (unique on org_id,campaign_id,target_type,target_id,attribution_type). 21 report_crm_* views following the established operations report pattern (§-canonical, see v117 §154 fact-view note): all security_invoker=true so org scope comes from the base tables' RLS, GRANT SELECT to authenticated+service_role only (no anon, so not in any anon-revoke sweep). report_crm_campaign_roi counts attributed_leads from campaign_attribution rows with target_type='lead' AND attributed_deals/won_revenue from rows with target_type='deal' (joined to deals + deal_stages.is_won), so campaign ROI requires attribution at BOTH lead-capture and deal-conversion time. OperationsDashboard is a new page at the GUARDED route /operations/dashboard (RoleGuard allowedRoles brainwise_super_admin + SuperAdminSessionProvider, identical wrapper to every other /operations/* route, and the guard is the access boundary, do not ship the bare element): 4 KPI cards, 2 recharts BarCharts (navy #021F36 Total, orange #F5741A Weighted), 4 SimpleTables; reads the report_crm_* views via opsSupabase.from(view).select. **TWO BACKEND GAPS CAUGHT + FIXED.** (1) **NEW CONVENTION: every new operations table the UI inserts into directly needs org_id DEFAULT operations.current_org_id().** The 4 Phase 7/8 tables (campaigns, campaign_attribution, lead_scoring_rules, workflow_rules) were created WITHOUT the org_id default that older ops tables carry (accounts/customers/etc. default operations.current_org_id()); the CRM create dialogs insert directly under RLS and omit org_id, so an insert would fail NOT NULL. Migration s122_p8_orgid_default_backfill set DEFAULT operations.current_org_id() on all four. STANDING CONVENTION going forward: any operations table written by a direct client insert (not exclusively via a SECDEF RPC that supplies org_id) must declare org_id DEFAULT operations.current_org_id() at creation, alongside the four-policy RLS. (2) **Campaign attribution wiring (additive internal-helper pattern for service-role paths).** ops_auto_attribute_lead_utm (the Phase-8 public RPC) was orphaned (nothing called it) AND it is org-guarded (raises forbidden_cross_org when current_org_id() != the lead's org), so it cannot run on the service-role webhook ingest path (ops-webhook-lead-capture -> ops_ingest_captured_lead) where current_org_id() is null. Result: no campaign_attribution rows were ever created and report_crm_campaign_roi + the dashboard campaign view always read empty. Fix (s122_p8_campaign_attribution_wiring, fully additive, no existing RPC modified): internal operations._attribute_lead_utm(uuid) (SECDEF search_path '', NO current_org_id guard, derives org from the lead row, mirrors the public RPC's campaign match [lower(name)=lower(utm) OR custom_fields->>'utm_campaign'] + first_touch insert, idempotent via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING; REVOKE EXECUTE FROM authenticated/anon/PUBLIC + GRANT service_role per §156). Two triggers on operations.leads, both SECDEF trigger functions: AFTER INSERT tg_lead_attribute_on_insert (when utm_campaign present, attribute the captured lead to its campaign, covers webhook + manual + future import in one place) and AFTER UPDATE OF converted_deal_id tg_lead_attribution_to_deal (WHEN old null -> new not null, copies the lead's campaign_attribution rows to the new deal as target_type='deal', driving attributed_deals + won_revenue, firing regardless of which RPC performs the conversion). Public ops_auto_attribute_lead_utm kept as the manual re-attribution entry. This is the SAME shape as the Won-bridge org-guard problem: when an org-guarded public RPC's logic must also run on a service-role path, add an additive internal service-role helper that derives org from the row rather than trying to call the guarded RPC. Functional test (rolled back): seeded a sentinel campaign, captured a UTM lead (INSERT trigger -> 1 lead attribution), built a minimal deal and set converted_deal_id (UPDATE trigger -> 1 deal attribution), asserted report_crm_campaign_roi attributed_leads=1/attributed_deals=1; SENTINEL_OK, zero residue. **DASHBOARD COLUMN-KEY LESSON:** Lovable guessed table column keys that did not exist in the views (total_deals/won_deals, source, lost_value); verified against information_schema.columns and corrected to the real keys (deals_reached/deals_won, source_name, lost_amount). When wiring a frontend table to a SQL view, verify the column names against the live view, never trust a generated guess. **Edge fn versions: NONE changed this session** (ops-webhook-lead-capture v1 was read only, to diagnose the attribution gap; it normalizes UTMs into the lead but never invoked the attribution RPC). Cron slots in use: jobids 1-32. ops-stripe-webhook (be435d9f) / platform stripe-webhook (fb9725d2) never cross-modified. *v123 - Session 121 CLOSE. **Operations Doc-2 CRM Phases 5 (Calendar) and 6 (Lead capture + enrichment) COMPLETE and verified (backend + frontend).** Backend-first; every apply_migration followed by a separate execute_sql verification; every functional test a single rolled-back DO block (sentinel RAISE, zero residue); all four new Edge Functions boot-verified (no-secret/perimeter to 401/400, correct path to 200); all frontend verified by GitHub API SHA. **NEW STANDING RULE §157:** this Supabase instance's default privileges auto-GRANT to authenticated on newly created TABLES (the table-level analog of §156's function behaviour). For a secret-bearing table, enabling RLS with no authenticated policy hides the rows but the privilege still exists; lock it with an explicit REVOKE ALL ON <table> FROM authenticated, anon and verify has_table_privilege('authenticated', ..., 'SELECT') = false plus zero authenticated/anon rows in information_schema.role_column_grants. Applied to operations.lead_capture_webhooks (carries hmac_secret). §1 to §156 hold. **PHASE 5: CALENDAR / REMINDERS.** organizations gained timezone (default America/New_York), day_of_digest_hour (default 8, 0-23 CHECK), reminders_enabled (default true). Two tables, audit-log posture (SELECT-only RLS own-org, writes via service_role SECDEF): operations.meeting_calendar_links (org_id default current_org_id FK RESTRICT, activity_id FK CASCADE, generated_by_user_id FK users SET NULL, output_format CHECK google|outlook_web|outlook_desktop|ics) and operations.meeting_reminders (activity_id FK CASCADE NOT NULL, reminder_type CHECK 1hr_before|day_of_digest|15min_app_notify, scheduled_for_at, sent_at, sent_to_user_id FK users SET NULL, delivery_method/delivery_status; UNIQUE(activity_id, reminder_type, sent_to_user_id) = the dedup backstop). Public SECDEF RPCs (search_path ''): ops_record_calendar_link(p_activity,p_output_format) (authenticated+service_role; validates the meeting is in current_org, stamps generated_by_user_id=auth.uid()); ops_record_meeting_reminder_sent / ops_record_day_of_digest_sent / ops_due_meeting_reminders / ops_due_day_of_digest (service_role-only, §156-locked off authenticated); ops_update_reminder_settings(p_patch) (authenticated+service_role, admin-gated, validates the timezone by attempting now() AT TIME ZONE and the hour 0-23). The two selectors run in cron context (no JWT, so they iterate orgs directly rather than via current_org_id) and RETURN fully rendered branded subject+body_html (navy/orange) so the edge fns are dumb senders. ops_due_meeting_reminders picks meetings with scheduled_start_at in (now+45min, now+60min], not all_day, status<>'done', completed_at null, owner has an email, reminders_enabled, and NOT EXISTS a meeting_reminders dedup row. ops_due_day_of_digest self-gates on extract(hour from now() at org.timezone)=day_of_digest_hour, aggregates today's (org-local-date) meeting/call/task items per owner, only emits when at least one item, and dedups via a 'day_of_digest_sent' audit_log event dated today-in-org-tz (the digest is multi-activity so it does NOT write meeting_reminders). The 15min_app_notify enum value exists for forward-compat but is never written (no ops in-app notification surface in v1). Crons: jobid 28 ops_meeting_reminder_cron 5,20,35,50 (every 15 min, offset off the */15 pile) and jobid 29 ops_day_of_digest_cron hourly :10 (the org-local-hour gate makes it DST-safe without a fixed UTC slot). A real bug (GET DIAGNOSTICS ROW_COUNT assigned into a boolean var) was caught by the functional DO-block and fixed body-only. **PHASE 6: LEAD CAPTURE + ENRICHMENT.** Three tables. operations.lead_capture_webhooks (org_id default current_org_id FK RESTRICT, name, recipe CHECK generic|lovable_form|tally|microsoft_bookings|stripe|zapier, public_token UNIQUE default hex(16 random bytes), hmac_secret default hex(32 random bytes), require_signature default true, auto_enrich default false, rate_limit_per_min default 60, default_lead_source_id FK picklist SET NULL, field_mapping jsonb, is_active, last_received_at, total_received, audit cols; set_updated_at trigger; RLS enabled with NO authenticated policy AND REVOKE ALL FROM authenticated/anon per §157; all access via SECDEF RPCs so the secret is privilege-hidden). operations.webhook_ingestion_log (org_id FK SET NULL, webhook_id FK SET NULL, source_ip, received_at, outcome CHECK accepted|rejected_signature|rejected_inactive|rejected_unknown|honeypot|throttled|error|duplicate, lead_id FK SET NULL, detail, payload_excerpt jsonb; indexes (webhook_id,received_at desc)/(source_ip,received_at desc)/(org_id,received_at desc) for the rate-limit window; SELECT-own-org RLS + authenticated read). operations.enrichment_log = the queue (org_id FK RESTRICT, lead_id FK CASCADE, contact_id FK CASCADE, provider CHECK apollo|hunter, enrichment_kind CHECK organization|email_verify|person, status CHECK pending|done|error|throttled|skipped default pending, attempts, input jsonb, result jsonb, error_detail, requested_by_user_id FK SET NULL, enqueued_at, processed_at; *v122 - Session 120 CLOSE. Operations Doc-2 CRM Phase 4 (Email Sync-A) COMPLETE and verified. No new standing rule (§1 to §156 hold). Backend-first; every apply_migration followed by a separate execute_sql verification; every functional test a single rolled-back DO block (sentinel RAISE, zero residue); both new Edge Functions boot-verified; all frontend verified by GitHub API SHA. Scope was compose-and-send outbound plus BCC/forward inbound logging; there is NO two-way OAuth and no "Sync-B". **FINDING, naming collision:** operations.email_templates ALREADY EXISTS (the Doc-1 invoice/reminder templates keyed by template_type), so the CRM template library is a SEPARATE table operations.crm_email_templates (name, category, subject, body_html, body_text, merge_tags_used text[], is_active, created_by/updated_by FK auth.users SET NULL). The frontend manages it via direct opsSupabase CRUD (no CRUD RPCs). **AUDIT-LOG POSTURE (reuses the §-substrate from Phase 7 / §156).** Three new write-once tables. operations.email_activities (FK activities ON DELETE CASCADE; from/to/cc/bcc[]; subject/body; resend_message_id with a partial-unique index; sent_at; send_status CHECK queued|sent|failed; send_error; opened/clicked counters with first/last timestamps; unsubscribed_at; template_id FK crm_email_templates SET NULL; merge_data jsonb). operations.email_tracking_events (append-only: email_activity_id FK CASCADE, event_type CHECK open|click|unsubscribe|bounce|complaint|delivered, event_at, ip_address, user_agent, link_url; dedup unique index on (email_activity_id, event_type, event_at, coalesce(link_url,''))). operations.email_inbound_ingestion (received_for_user_id FK users SET NULL, resend_inbound_id partial-unique, from_address, to/cc arrays, subject, body_html/text, received_at, match_status CHECK matched|unmatched default unmatched, matched_contact_id FK contact_persons SET NULL, activity_id FK activities SET NULL, raw jsonb). All three carry a SELECT-only RLS policy (authenticated, own-org) with NO write policy; every write routes through a SECDEF recorder run by service_role, so the authenticated grants Supabase auto-applies are inert against the RLS. **OUTBOUND.** Two public SECDEF RPCs (search_path '', §156-locked authenticated plus service_role). ops_crm_email_prepare(p_payload) enforces opt-out (transactional_opt_out is a hard block; marketing_opt_out with send_type in templated|bulk|marketing is a block; marketing with one_off is a warning list), matches recipients (to union cc union bcc, lowercased) against contact_persons in-org, and returns the render_merge'd subject and body plus matched_contact_ids plus marketing_warning_addresses. ops_crm_email_record_sent(p_payload) writes the activities row (type='email', optional related_to, inline email_* columns, owner is the sender resolved from operations.users by auth.uid()) plus the email_activities row plus log_activity('email_sent' or 'email_send_failed'). The composer always sends send_type='one_off' (templated and bulk are reserved for future sequences). Tracking recorder public.ops_crm_email_record_tracking(resend_message_id, event_type, event_at, link_url, ip, user_agent) is service_role-ONLY: it maps Resend event names to the CHECK set, finds the email_activities row by resend_message_id (returns false for a non-CRM message, so it self-filters), inserts the tracking event inside a BEGIN/EXCEPTION unique_violation-to-false guard (retry dedup), and increments the open/click counters plus stamps activities.email_opened_at/clicked_at. **INBOUND.** The routing key is operations.users.inbox_token (24 hex chars from extensions.gen_random_bytes(12), backfilled distinct, then DEFAULT plus NOT NULL plus UNIQUE); each user's address is the token concatenated with '@inbox.brainwiseenterprises.com'. ops_get_my_inbox_address() (authenticated) returns {token, address}. Recorder public.ops_crm_email_record_inbound(p_payload) is service_role-ONLY: it resolves user plus org by inbox_token (ignored if the token is unknown), is idempotent on resend_inbound_id, ALWAYS stores the raw ingestion row, then best-effort matches a contact by from/to/cc (lowercased, minus the user's own address and the @inbox domain) and on a hit creates an activities row (type='email', related_to the contact) plus flips match_status to matched plus log_activity('email_received'). Manual link public.ops_crm_email_link_inbound(ingestion_id, entity_type, entity_id) (authenticated) attaches an unmatched row to a lead|account|contact|deal, creating the activity and setting matched plus activity_id, and logs 'email_linked'. **Sent and received emails surface in the existing ops_entity_timeline with NO RPC change** (it already returns every activity for an entity, and email activities are just type='email'). **EDGE FUNCTIONS.** crm-email-send v1 NEW (verify_jwt TRUE, caller-context anon client; prepare, then a Resend send from "BrainWise <crm@mail.brainwiseenterprises.com>", then record_sent; best-effort failed-record on a Resend error; boot-verified unauth to 401). crm-email-inbound v1 NEW (verify_jwt FALSE; Svix-verified using a SEPARATE secret RESEND_INBOUND_WEBHOOK_SECRET, distinct from the delivery-webhook secret; gate order is svix-header presence, then secret, then freshness, then verify; it handles the email.received metadata-only payload, extracts the token from any @inbox recipient, does a best-effort body fetch via npm:resend@4 receiving.get with a metadata-only fallback so the record is never lost, and calls record_inbound via a service-role client; boot-verified no-svix to 400 and bogus-sig to 401 after the secret was set). resend-webhook v12 (the SHARED platform Svix-verified delivery-events function; added one additive fail-soft block that calls ops_crm_email_record_tracking for every event via service-role, self-filtering non-CRM messages, and leaving the existing email_logs and newsletter paths untouched; perimeter re-verified no-svix to 400 and bogus-sig to 401). The ops and platform Stripe webhooks were never cross-modified. **FRONTEND (Lovable, all verified by GitHub API SHA).** ComposeEmailDialog.tsx (to/cc/bcc split on [,;], subject, body to body_text plus a simple body_html, a crm_email_templates picker; flow is supabase.rpc ops_crm_email_prepare, a marketing window.confirm on warnings, then functions.invoke crm-email-send). EntityTimeline.tsx (shared) gained a "Compose email" button beside "Log activity" plus an optional defaultEmail prop and a timeline-invalidate onSent. OperationsContactDetail.tsx passes defaultEmail from the contact. OperationsEmailTemplates.tsx (/operations/email-templates) is direct opsSupabase CRUD over crm_email_templates. OperationsInbound.tsx (/operations/inbound) is a forwarding-address card (ops_get_my_inbox_address plus a copy button) plus a filterable email_inbound_ingestion list (embedding matched_contact) with a contact-search link dialog calling ops_crm_email_link_inbound. Routes and sidebar entries (Email Templates with the Mail icon, Inbound with the Inbox icon) are additive in the CRM section. **INTENTIONAL v1 DEFERRALS:** attachments (inbound stores body only; the composer cannot attach), synchronous send (no retry queue), open-tracking off and clicks on (Cole's choice), the inbound manual-link UI targets contacts only although the RPC supports all four entity types, and a plain-text composer body. **COLE-SIDE CONFIG DONE:** the Resend email.received webhook to /functions/v1/crm-email-inbound and the RESEND_INBOUND_WEBHOOK_SECRET are set (perimeter confirmed by a 401 on a bad signature). PENDING (non-blocking): no real inbound row exists yet, so a live BCC/forward smoke test would exercise the one path not yet hit in production (the Resend SDK body-fetch). Edge fn versions at close: crm-email-send v1 NEW, crm-email-inbound v1 NEW, resend-webhook v12; all other ops and platform fns unchanged. Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v128, this v122 entry, session-120-to-121.md.*

Added operations.users.is_salesperson boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false. **Reusable seeder** `operations.seed_crm_defaults(p_org uuid) RETURNS jsonb` (SECDEF, search_path '', §156-locked: REVOKE EXECUTE FROM PUBLIC, anon, authenticated + GRANT service_role; verified has_function_privilege('authenticated', ...)=false) seeds default config idempotently (ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING on the unique keys), so it doubles as the org-creation seeding entry point at productization. All CRM tables: org_id DEFAULT current_org_id() FK organizations RESTRICT, set_updated_at trigger (except append-only stage_history), four-policy org-scoped RLS, authenticated + service_role grants. **Behavior:** two deals triggers — BEFORE INSERT/UPDATE `deals_set_probability_close` (probability follows the stage default on insert and on change unless the caller set it; actual_close_date stamped on a won/lost stage) and AFTER INSERT/UPDATE `deals_record_stage_history` (records every transition incl. the initial one, computes time_in_prior_stage_seconds, transitioned_by resolved via operations.users lookup of auth.uid() so non-ops/cron actors store null). Three public SECDEF RPCs (search_path '', REVOKE anon/PUBLIC, GRANT authenticated+service_role; verified anon=false/auth=true): `ops_convert_lead(p_lead_id,p_options jsonb)` (account resolution forced-id > email-domain match > new prospect; creates the contact created_from='lead_conversion', primary when the account has none; optional deal in the default pipeline's first open stage; archives the lead with conversion links; logs lead_converted + account_created_from_lead + deal_created), `ops_bulk_convert_leads(uuid[],jsonb)` (per-lead EXCEPTION isolation, returns converted/errors + counts), `ops_create_customer_from_deal(p_deal_id)` (Won bridge: idempotent on account.customer_id; else creates the customers row from the account, sets account.customer_id + type='customer', links the account's unlinked contacts; NO auto-on-Won trigger — that is Phase 7's 5-min-delay queue). Verified by one rolled-back DO block (JWT-sim as the ops admin): convert produced a new account + initial probability 10 + 1 stage-history row; a stage move to Discovery set probability 25 + a 2nd history row with non-null time-in-prior; the bridge created the customer, set account.customer_id, flipped type to customer, and linked the contact; sentinel RAISE rolled back with zero residue. **PHASE 2 SHIPPED (3 migrations) — activities + unified timeline.** `operations.activities` is a single discriminated table (type CHECK task|call|meeting|email|note) with allow-null CHECKs on status/priority/call_type/call_result, meeting + email_* columns inline (manually-logged emails work before Phase 4's full Sync-A email_activities), attachment_count, custom_fields, and a polymorphic related_to (related_to_type CHECK lead|account|contact|deal + related_to_id, guarded by a both-or-neither CHECK and by the BEFORE-trigger `activities_validate_related` which confirms the target row exists in the same org or raises). `operations.activity_attendees` (attendee_type contact|user|external, FKs SET NULL) and `operations.activity_attachments` (metadata only; the operations-attachments storage bucket per Doc 5 §3.2 is deferred to the Phase-3/upload UI) round it out; an AFTER trigger `activity_attachments_count` maintains activities.attachment_count. All three are RLS four-policy org-scoped with authenticated/service_role grants. `public.ops_entity_timeline(p_entity_type,p_entity_id,p_limit)` (SECDEF, search_path '', anon/PUBLIC revoked, authenticated+service_role) returns the unified chronological feed for a lead/account/contact/deal: a jsonb array UNIONing activities (matched on related_to) with audit_log events (matched on entity), each item {source,id,kind,at,subject,actor_user_id,details}, ordered desc with the limit applied inside the union BEFORE aggregation (an outer LIMIT on jsonb_agg would not cap items). `operations.deal_pipeline_health` (view, security_invoker) exposes per deal: is_open, days_in_current_stage (computed off the latest deal_stage_history transitioned_at, falling back to created_at), rot_threshold_days, is_rotting (open + threshold exceeded), next_activity_at + has_next_activity (earliest future, uncompleted task/call/meeting), and is_stale_no_activity (the Pipedrive activity-based-selling warn flag; false on terminal stages). Verified by one rolled-back DO block (JWT-sim admin): related-to bad-ref raised; attachment_count 1 then 0; ops_entity_timeline returned both an activity and an audit event; deal_pipeline_health showed has_next=true / stale=false / open=true / rotting=false; zero residue. **PHASE 3 P3.1 (Lovable, frontend) SHIPPED + verified by API SHA (commit 5a8e29b).** Recon established the live operations frontend conventions: pages in src/pages/operations/, routes in src/App.tsx (RoleGuard allowedRoles brainwise_super_admin + SuperAdminSessionProvider), nav in src/components/AppSidebar.tsx (typed NavItem array + sectionHeader), the opsSupabase-for-tables / supabase.rpc-as-any-for-RPCs client split, operations-types.ts not regenerated (use `.from("x" as any)` + embeds), list template OperationsCustomers.tsx, shared helpers in _shared.tsx. *v120 - Session 118 CLOSE — Operations Doc-1 Phase 8 (customer depth + Zoho migration) COMPLETE. No new standing rule (§1–§156 hold). Backend-first throughout; every functional test a single rolled-back DO block (sentinel RAISE, zero residue); both Lovable prompts verified against the repo by API SHA. **New read surface — operations.customer_account_summary** (view, security_invoker=true; GRANT SELECT authenticated+service_role, no anon): per customer — outstanding_balance + open_invoice_count (from customer_balance_summary), unused_credit_amount + open_credit_count (count of customer_credits with available_balance>0). Drives the customer-detail header chips. **Contact-persons CRUD** (public SECDEF search_path '', anon/PUBLIC revoked, authenticated+service_role; org-scoped via current_org_id()): ops_list_contacts(p_customer_id), ops_add_contact(p_customer_id,p_payload jsonb)→uuid, ops_update_contact(p_id,p_payload jsonb) (partial via the p_payload ? key test), ops_delete_contact(p_id) (hard delete — contact_persons has no FK children). Primary-flag exclusivity enforced on add+update (at most one is_primary per customer); cross-org guards; every write logs activity on the PARENT customer (entity_type='customer'). **Customer statement — public.ops_customer_statement(p_customer_id,p_from date,p_to date,p_unpaid_only bool)→jsonb** (SECDEF, org-scoped). Ledger model: invoice = debit (total_amount, excl draft/void); payment = credit (amount − refunded_amount); credit-note = credit (total_amount, excl void); customer_credits is deliberately NOT a ledger source (avoids double-counting against credit-notes). Returns {customer, from, to, unpaid_only, opening_balance (null in unpaid-only mode), closing_balance, total_outstanding, transactions[{date,type,number,description,debit,credit,balance}] with a running balance via a window fn, open_invoices[]}. **Generic CSV import RPCs** (public SECDEF): ops_import_customers(p_rows jsonb, p_mode 'dry_run'|'commit', p_on_conflict 'skip'|'update')→jsonb and ops_import_items(...). The client maps CSV→normalized keys; conflict key lower(display_name) / sku-else-name; bad type/status/numeric → warning+default, missing required → per-row error; returns {mode,on_conflict,total,counts:{insert,update,skip,error},rows[…]}. The RPCs are live; the planned generic import-wizard UI (Prompt 3) was NOT shipped and is SUPERSEDED for the present need (one real customer migrated by script instead). **Frontend (Lovable, both prompts verified against the repo):** OperationsCustomerDetail.tsx rebuilt to a 9-tab shadcn layout (Projects / Invoices / Estimates / Payments / Credit Notes / Account Credit / Expenses / Contacts / Statement) + account-summary header chips + a time rollup; new ContactFormDialog.tsx wired to the contact RPCs (useEffect-seeded edit buffer, primary checkbox). documentPdf.ts gained a StatementData type + generateStatementPdf / downloadStatementPdf (reuses the existing PDF helpers; ledger table when !unpaid_only, open-invoices always, footer on page breaks); the Statement tab has date inputs + an unpaid-only Switch + Generate (ops_customer_statement) + Download PDF, with `today` built from local date parts (§116, no toISOString). **NEW REUSABLE PATTERN — scripted one-time data ingest (Zoho migration).** For a single-customer historical load, a scripted idempotent purge+ingest is the right tool, NOT a UI importer. Shape: (1) recon the exact target footprint; (2) build the load as one DO block — idempotency guard on a source id stored in custom_fields (e.g. custom_fields->>'zoho_customer_id'); wire parent→child inserts with INSERT…SELECT FROM (VALUES …) joined on natural/source keys (lines→invoices on invoice_number; allocations→payments via the source id parked in notes); store every source id in custom_fields / notes for traceability; keep the source document numbers as free-text so the operations numbering sequence is untouched (no next_number consumed); (3) DRY-RUN the whole purge+ingest in a rolled-back block that RAISEs a sentinel carrying the post-state counts/totals, then run the identical block with the RAISE removed to commit, then re-verify live. This session migrated one real customer this way (customer + sole contact + 8 invoices + 29 free_form lines + 8 payments + 8 allocations, then 6 projects + 26 tasks + 45 time entries), after purging all org-scoped test transactional data (config untouched). Historical payment modes were bank/cash (no Stripe), so imported payments raise no Stripe-source-of-truth conflict. Imported invoices are standalone free_form documents — NOT linked to imported time entries or the items catalog. CAVEAT (recorded in the queue): the supplied timesheet export was partial vs the project hour summaries (97.00h ingested vs ~126.33h), so time-log views under-read Zoho's totals on 3 projects; billing is unaffected (captured in the invoices). VERIFY-QUERY LESSON (re-confirmed): a per-project roll-up that LEFT JOINs both project_tasks and time_entries to projects fans out (tasks × entries) and inflates count/sum — use scalar subqueries (or aggregate each child separately) for multi-child verification. **PHASE 8 COMPLETE**; Phase 9 (QA/polish/deploy) is next. Close artifacts (markdown only, Session-74): build-queue v126, this v120 entry, session-118-to-119.md.*

Internal helper operations.log_activity(p_org,p_entity_type,p_entity_id,p_action,p_details,p_actor_user,p_actor_external) (SECDEF search_path '') is the single audit writer; called by other SECDEF RPCs as owner and by service_role (cron/edge). Verified: forced-rollback DO-block test (sentinel-exception rollback, zero residue, zero numbering consumed) confirmed add→auto-log→read round-trip and correct org/actor resolution. **§156 NEW — internal SECDEF helpers need an explicit REVOKE EXECUTE FROM authenticated, not just FROM anon, PUBLIC.** This Supabase instance has default privileges that auto-GRANT EXECUTE on newly-created functions to the `authenticated` role, so `REVOKE ... FROM anon, PUBLIC` leaves a privilege-bearing-parameter helper (log_activity takes p_org + p_actor and is SECURITY DEFINER → a direct authenticated caller could forge audit rows for any org/actor) still callable by authenticated. Verify every new internal helper with has_function_privilege('authenticated', oid, 'EXECUTE') = false after the revoke; if true, add REVOKE FROM authenticated explicitly. Generalizes the existing comma-form-REVOKE rule: the comma form removes the inherited PUBLIC grant but NOT the default-privilege direct grant to authenticated. (Public-facing read/write RPCs are unaffected — they intentionally keep the authenticated grant.) **Sub-area 2 COMPLETE — server-side merge-tag renderer + email-template CRUD + reminder retrofit.** Rendering lives in SQL, not the edge layer (one renderer reused by reminders, in-app preview, and any future invoice-send template-ification; the edge fn is a dumb sender). operations.render_merge(p_text,p_context jsonb) (IMMUTABLE, search_path '', locked anon/PUBLIC/authenticated per §156, service_role only) replaces {{token}} with context->>token and BLANKS unresolved tokens so no raw {{x}} reaches a customer; replacement values have backslashes escaped first so a value can't be read as a regexp backreference. public.ops_get_merge_tag_catalog() returns the valid token set per template_type for the settings UI. Seeded one is_default active template per org for reminder_before_due / reminder_on_due / reminder_after_due / invoice_send / payment_receipt (idempotent one-per-(org,type); navy #021F36 / orange #F5741A button styling).
